-----title
博兴（博昌）
-----detail

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=649&endYear=649')">649年</a>　居青州博昌.始与当地文士有交往.《秋晨同淄州毛司马秋九咏》组诗作于本年及此后数年中。<span id='poem_sentence_2_42099'>盖阴连凤阙，阵影翼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_42099", 42099, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>龙城</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42103'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1039, "poem_sentence_3_42103")'>下帷</span>如不倦，当解<span id='poem_sentence_4_42103_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_42102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42102?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_42102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42102'>金翘徒可泛，玉斝竟谁同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=650&endYear=650')">650年</a>　居青州博昌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=651&endYear=651')">651年</a>　父死,葬之于博昌.奉母前往瑕丘。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='29ce6949fda2472fb78bda603befaedb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("29ce6949fda2472fb78bda603befaedb");'><span id='29ce6949fda2472fb78bda603befaedb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年</a>，46岁</div><div id='29ce6949fda2472fb78bda603befaedb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年</a>　赴临海任,经鲁地,有《与博昌父老书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第289页。）</span><div id='poem_1364275' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364275' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364275?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与博昌父老书</a><span class='authorDate'>（680年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364275")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364275_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364275'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364275'>月日。骆宾王致书于博昌父老等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364275_comment'></div>承并无恙。幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364275_comment'></div>云雨俄别。封壤异乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364275_comment'></div>春渚青山。载劳延想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364275_comment'></div>秋天白露。几变光阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364275_comment'></div>古人云。别易会难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364275_comment'></div>不其然也。自解携襟袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364275_comment'></div>一十五年。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364275", 1364275, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>交臂</span>存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364275_comment'></div>略无半在。张学士溘从朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364275_comment'></div>辟闾公倏掩夜台。故吏门人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364275_comment'></div>多游蒿里。耆年宿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364275_comment'></div>但见松邱。呜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364275_comment'></div>泉壤殊途。幽明永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364275_comment'></div>人理危促。天道奚言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364275_comment'></div>感今怀旧。不觉涕之无从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364275_comment'></div>过隙不留。藏舟难固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364275_comment'></div>追维逝者。浮生几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364275_comment'></div>哀缘物兴。事因情感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364275_comment'></div>虽蒙庄一指。殆先觉于劳生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364275_comment'></div>秦佚三号。讵忘情于怛化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364275_comment'></div>啜其泣矣。尚何云哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364275_comment'></div>又闻移县就乐安故城。廨宇邑居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364275_comment'></div>咸徙其地。里开阡陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364275_comment'></div>徒有其名。荒径三秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364275_comment'></div>蔓草滋于旧馆。颓墉四望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364275_comment'></div>拱木多于故人。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364275_comment'></div>仙鹤来归。辽东之城郭犹是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364275_comment'></div>灵乌代谢。汉南之陵谷已非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364275_comment'></div>昔吾先君。出宰斯邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364275_comment'></div>清芬虽远。遗爱犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364275_comment'></div>延首城池。何心天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364275_comment'></div>虽则山河四塞。是称无棣之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364275_comment'></div>松槚千秋。有切惟桑之里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364275_comment'></div>故每怀夙昔。尚想经过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364275_comment'></div>于役不遑。愿言徒拥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364275_comment'></div>今西成有岁。东户无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364275_comment'></div>野老清谈。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364275", 1364275, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>怡然自得</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364275_comment'></div>田家浊酒。乐以忘忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364275_comment'></div>故可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364275", 1364275, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>洽赏</span>当年。相欢卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364275_comment'></div>宁复<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364275", 1364275, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>惠存</span>旧好。追思昔游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364275_comment'></div>所恨企予望之。经途密迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364275_comment'></div>伫中衢而空轸。巾下泽而莫因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364275_comment'></div>风月虚心。形留神送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364275_comment'></div>山川在目。室迩人遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364275_comment'></div>以此怀劳。增其叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364275_comment'></div>情不遗旧。书何尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364275_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1364275_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
兖州（瑕丘）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fff51af55732421496b5596aad814d74_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fff51af55732421496b5596aad814d74");'><span id='fff51af55732421496b5596aad814d74_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=653&endYear=653')">653年</a>　居瑕丘。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0763b53127f0447d93b1d7c4aa1ed3cc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=656&endYear=656')">656年</a>　居瑕丘.有《夏日游德州赠高四并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷1第16页。）</span><div id='poem_42178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日游德州赠高四</a><span class='authorDate'>（656年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42178")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_42178_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_42178'>夫在心为志，发言为诗，诗有不得尽言，言有不得尽意。仆少负不羁，长逾虚诞，读书颇存涉猎，学剑不待穷工，进不能矫翰龙云，退不能栖神豹雾，抚循诸己，深觉劳生。而太夫人在堂，义须捧檄，因仰长安而就日，赴帝乡以望云。虽文阙三冬，而书劳十上。嗟乎，入门自媚，谁相谓言，致使君门隔于九重，中堂远于千里，既而交非得兔，路是亡羊，敬止弊庐，朅来初服，遂得载披玉叶，款洽金兰，倾意气于一言，缔风期于千祀。虽交因气合，资得意以敦交，道契言忘，少寄言而筌道，是以轻投木李，以代疏麻，章句繁芜，心神愧恧，庶瞻雅韵，伫辱报章，则紫耀运星，开龙文于剑匣，素辉亏月，领骊颔于珠胎云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_42178_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42178'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(11, onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8871, "poem_sentence_14_42178")'>吴起</span>，思赵切廉颇。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42178'>凄断<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3741, "poem_sentence_15_42178")'>韩王剑</span>，生死<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1010, "poem_sentence_15_42178")'>翟公罗</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42178'>罗悲翟公意，剑负韩王气。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42178'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_42178", 42178, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>骄饵</span>去易论，忌途良可畏。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42178'>夙昔怀江海，平生混<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2915, "poem_sentence_18_42178")'>泾渭</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_42178'>千载契风云，一言忘贱贵。<div id='poem_sentence_19_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_42178'>去去访林泉，空谷有遗贤。<div id='poem_sentence_20_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_42178'>言投<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_42178", 42178, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>爵里刺</span>，来泛<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9753, "poem_sentence_21_42178")'>野人船</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_21_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_42178'>缔交君<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_22_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_42178'>成风<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(233, "poem_sentence_23_42178")'><span "poem_sentence_23_42178")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_42178", 42178, "Clauses/47/Comments/1")'>伯牙弦</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_25_42178'>聊安<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3802, "poem_sentence_25_42178")'>张蔚庐</span>，讵扫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_42178", 42178, id='poem_sentence_45_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_42178'>野衣裁薜叶，山酒酌藤花。<div id='poem_sentence_46_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_42178'>白云离望远，青溪隐路赊。<div id='poem_sentence_47_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_42178'>傥忆幽岩桂，犹冀折<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_42178", 42178, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>疏麻</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_48_42178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_1364282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364282?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上兖州刺史启</a><span class='authorDate'>（665年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364282")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364282'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364282'>侧闻未遇孙阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364282_comment'></div>盐车无绝尘之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364282_comment'></div>时逢和氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364282_comment'></div>荆山有连城之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364282_comment'></div>岂若听清音于爨馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364282_comment'></div>则枯桐发响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364282_comment'></div>收夜光于元璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364282_comment'></div>则怪石腾辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364282_comment'></div>在物犹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364282_comment'></div>况于含识者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364282_comment'></div>伏惟明使君凤穴振仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364282_comment'></div>龙门标峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364282_comment'></div>琼雕岳立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364282_comment'></div>表秀干云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364282_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>霞焕</span>霜霏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364282_comment'></div>澄虚鉴物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364282_comment'></div>既而代工天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364282_comment'></div>忠简帝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364282_comment'></div>拥熊轼而抚百城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364282_comment'></div>建隼旟而临千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364282_comment'></div>坐棠敷惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364282_comment'></div>恩缠去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364282_comment'></div>剖竹垂仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364282_comment'></div>式歌来暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364282_comment'></div>清凝夜烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364282_comment'></div>化警晨乌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364282_comment'></div>外勖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>九农</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364282_comment'></div>内宏五教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364282_comment'></div>道之以礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364282_comment'></div>齐之以刑书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364282_comment'></div>约法遵宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364282_comment'></div>设蒲鞭之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364282_comment'></div>立言惟信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364282_comment'></div>控竹马之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364282_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>甘雨随车</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364282_comment'></div>云低轻重之盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364282_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>还珠合浦</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364282_comment'></div>波含远近之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364282_comment'></div>至如卧理称难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364282_comment'></div>坐啸匪易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364282_comment'></div>披裳问疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364282_comment'></div>垂爱景以字人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364282_comment'></div>搴帷广听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364282_comment'></div>穆薰风而扇物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364282_comment'></div>飞霜秋降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364282_comment'></div>叶隼击而防小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364282_comment'></div>零露春濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364282_comment'></div>饰羔旌而礼君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364282_comment'></div>于是仁必有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364282_comment'></div>吏不忍欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364282_comment'></div>美誉郁于三齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364282_comment'></div>芳声腾于万古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364282_comment'></div>若乃清规远镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364282_comment'></div>皎月色于灵台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364282_comment'></div>元鉴虚凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364282_comment'></div>穆松风于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>智府</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364282_comment'></div>研几十箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364282_comment'></div>探颐九流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364282_comment'></div>缛翠萼于词林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364282_comment'></div>綷仙花于笔苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364282_comment'></div>文江翻浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364282_comment'></div>织<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>玉潋</span>以韬霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364282_comment'></div>学海惊澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364282_comment'></div>缀珠连于濯锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364282_comment'></div>加以悬榻待士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364282_comment'></div>拥彗礼贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364282_comment'></div>汲引忘疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364282_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>奖题</span>不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364282_comment'></div>怀经味道之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364282_comment'></div>望范围而骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364282_comment'></div>兼流包略之夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364282_comment'></div>窥义园以遐集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364282_comment'></div>求小善于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>毫芥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364282_comment'></div>顾正礼于二龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364282_comment'></div>振幽滞于泥沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364282_comment'></div>许公明以一骥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364282_comment'></div>某淹中故俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364282_comment'></div>体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>朴厚</span>之清规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364282_comment'></div>稷下遗氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364282_comment'></div>陶礼义之馀化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364282_comment'></div>颇游<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>简素</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364282_comment'></div>少阅<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>缣缃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364282_comment'></div>每蟋蟀凄吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364282_comment'></div>映素雪于书帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364282_comment'></div>莎鸡振羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364282_comment'></div>截碧蒲于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>翰池</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364282_comment'></div>既而学异<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_86_1364282", 1364282, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>怀蛟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364282_comment'></div>才非梦鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364282_comment'></div>价不齐于南汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364282_comment'></div>芳不重于东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364282_comment'></div>幸属日月光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364282_comment'></div>云霞纷郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364282_comment'></div>方结羡鱼之网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364282_comment'></div>将谣扣角之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364282_comment'></div>奋短翮于枪榆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364282_comment'></div>希高标之馀拂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364282_comment'></div>濯纤鳞于涓滴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364282_comment'></div>望鸿泽之微沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364282_comment'></div>所冀顾盼曲流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364282_comment'></div>剪拂增价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364282_comment'></div>则铅刀起一割之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364282_comment'></div>跛鳖致千里之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364282_comment'></div>是知窃混吹于齐竽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364282_comment'></div>滥飞声于郢唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364282_comment'></div>抱山鸡而自恧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364282_comment'></div>顾辽豕以多惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364282_comment'></div>轻触威严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364282_comment'></div>不遑流汗。<div class='inline' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364283'>侧闻丰城戢耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364283_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364283", 1364283, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>骇电</span>之辉俄剖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364283_comment'></div>沙邱踠迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364283_comment'></div>蹑云之辔载驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364283_comment'></div>然则激溜侵星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364283_comment'></div>佩潜蛟于壮武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364283_comment'></div>腾镳历块。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364283_comment'></div>骋蹀骏于咸阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364283_comment'></div>且煦辙波鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364283_comment'></div>侧羡鳌潭之跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364283_comment'></div>触笼云翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364283_comment'></div>扃望鹏程之迅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364283_comment'></div>是以齐郊夕唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364283_comment'></div>牛歌掞白石之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364283_comment'></div>汉境朝趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364283_comment'></div>车候警拂尘之思。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1364283_comment'></div>擢干捎云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364283_comment'></div>翊孤岩而耸桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364283_comment'></div>崇基謺秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364283_comment'></div>匡霸道于周盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364283_comment'></div>茂绪联辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364283_comment'></div>灵台宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364283_comment'></div>骋霄练于霜潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364283_comment'></div>册府幽深。<div id='poem_sentence_32_1364283_comment'></div>泳耀魄于黄陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364283_comment'></div>情岳干天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364283_comment'></div>韬风云于嵇巘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364283_comment'></div>龙津共济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364283_comment'></div>竞欣登御之车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364283_comment'></div>芜室钦贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364283_comment'></div>必揽澄清之辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364283_comment'></div>郁文条而耀彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364283_comment'></div>藻逸潘花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364283_comment'></div>蔚词锋而衒奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364283_comment'></div>光浮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364283", 1364283, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>卫玉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364283_comment'></div>然则昆溪既琢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364283_comment'></div>必见山川之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364283_comment'></div>树羽已悬。<div showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上兖州张司马启</a><span class='authorDate'>（665年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364284'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364284'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364284_comment'></div>窃闻网涧缉裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364284_comment'></div>傃指云于偃盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364284_comment'></div>排虚止棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364284_comment'></div>附绝电于纤离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364284_comment'></div>然则左右为容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364284_comment'></div>锵金有阶于蟠木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364284_comment'></div>无因而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364284_comment'></div>桉剑致惧于连城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364284_comment'></div>是以赁牍干荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364284_comment'></div>发仞资于禽息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364284_comment'></div>求光抱燧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364284_comment'></div>束发济于于瞢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364284_comment'></div>伏惟某官琼峰耸峭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364284_comment'></div>俨曦观而争峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364284_comment'></div>瑶派惊澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364284_comment'></div>溯天潢而比浚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364284_comment'></div>汉台引路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364284_comment'></div>夕翊浮云之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364284_comment'></div>晋閤垂珰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364284_comment'></div>朝煜文星之苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364284_comment'></div>剑池濯彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364284_comment'></div>耀震德于渥津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364284_comment'></div>弱水摛祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364284_comment'></div>炫离精于丹穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364284_comment'></div>辨悬瞳于朗镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364284_comment'></div>肇自觿年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364284_comment'></div>对似魄于亏阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364284_comment'></div>光乎弱岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364284_comment'></div>言阿激箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364284_comment'></div>浴紫贝以飞湍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364284_comment'></div>情岳惊峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364284_comment'></div>蔽丹霄而杰峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364284_comment'></div>文条擢秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364284_comment'></div>馥长坂之幽兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364284_comment'></div>笔苑扬葩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364284_comment'></div>煜小山之丹桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364284_comment'></div>松飙结韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364284_comment'></div>搢绅藉以雌黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364284_comment'></div>嵓电流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364284_comment'></div>通贤资其月旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364284_comment'></div>于是佐褰帷于鲁甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364284_comment'></div>威詟列藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364284_comment'></div>匡露冕于梁阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364284_comment'></div>恩覃绝境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364284_comment'></div>缉谐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364284", 1364284, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>麟甸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364284_comment'></div>下白鹤于仙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364284_comment'></div>辅弼凫郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364284_comment'></div>重黄金于帝里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364284_comment'></div>加以奖拔幽滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364284_comment'></div>汲引英髦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364284_comment'></div>锡以吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364284_comment'></div>暖燕郊之阴谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364284_comment'></div>延之顾盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364284_comment'></div>焰汉圄之寒灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364284_comment'></div>某筱派庸微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364284_comment'></div>桐岩贱伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364284_comment'></div>托根邹邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364284_comment'></div>时闻阙里之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364284_comment'></div>接闬雩津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364284_comment'></div>屡听杏坛之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364284_comment'></div>加以承<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364284", 1364284, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>断织</span>之慈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364284_comment'></div>得锐志于书林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364284_comment'></div>奉过庭之严规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364284_comment'></div>遂容情于义圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364284_comment'></div>方欲闭门却扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364284_comment'></div>养拙以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364284", 1364284, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>终年</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364284_comment'></div>幽遁凿坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364284_comment'></div>甘贫而卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364284_comment'></div>直以栖迟五亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364284_comment'></div>获鹪鹩之数粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364284_comment'></div>萧条三径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364284_comment'></div>匮侏儒之斗储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364284_comment'></div>虽则放旷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1364284", 1364284, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>林泉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364284_comment'></div>颇得閒居之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364284_comment'></div>而乃寂寞蓬户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364284_comment'></div>唯深色养之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364284_comment'></div>是以望檄动容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364284_comment'></div>慨南阳而闻寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364284_comment'></div>祈名夙驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364284_comment'></div>叹郢路而依迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364284_comment'></div>方今凉秋届节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364284_comment'></div>严飙扇序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364284_comment'></div>衡阳极浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364284_comment'></div>振朝音于负霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364284_comment'></div>寒皋回甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364284_comment'></div>惊宵吟于静野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364284_comment'></div>弓旌之礼斯及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364284_comment'></div>辟聘之际是期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364284_comment'></div>不揆庸愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364284_comment'></div>轻斯自衒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364284_comment'></div>所冀分其末照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364284_comment'></div>惠以馀波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364284_comment'></div>得预观光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364284_comment'></div>全由咳唾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364284_comment'></div>倘云镳释绁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364284_comment'></div>申其漱玉之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364284_comment'></div>霜匣开辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364284_comment'></div>照以盘蛟之影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364284_comment'></div>则阴山之雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364284_comment'></div>敢怀餐蕊之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364284_comment'></div>汉东之蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364284_comment'></div>期致投珠之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364284_comment'></div>不胜窘迫之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364284_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1364284_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上梁明府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（665年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364288")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364288'>窃闻薛邑闻琴。揖冯谖于弹铗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364288_comment'></div>夷门伫驾。顾侯嬴于抱关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364288_comment'></div>何则。志合风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364288_comment'></div>戴笠均乎乘马。情谐道术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364288_comment'></div>忘筌贵乎得鱼。是用挹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364288", 1364288, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>兰言</span>于断金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364288_comment'></div>效蓬心于匪石。庶清音动听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364288_comment'></div>赏流水于牙弦。妙思通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364288_comment'></div>叶薰风于郢匠。伏惟某公仪天峙构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364288_comment'></div>层基控射牛之峰。浸地开源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364288_comment'></div>惊涛疏钓鳌之浦。至夫封侯庙食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364288_comment'></div>掩金张以骞翥。三主七公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364288_comment'></div>罩袁扬而岳立。故得重规远镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364288_comment'></div>湛月露以流清。茂趾霞铺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364288_comment'></div>驾云门而擢秀。若乃博闻强记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364288_comment'></div>辨晋国之黄熊。将圣多能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364288_comment'></div>识吴门之白马。言泉漱迥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364288_comment'></div>惊瀑布以飞澜。文江澹虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364288_comment'></div>涵濯锦而翻浪。于是功超<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364288", 1364288, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>食蹠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364288_comment'></div>位典烹鲜。水镜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364288", 1364288, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>澄澜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364288_comment'></div>照孤鸾之舞影。鸣琴动操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364288_comment'></div>叶驯翚之雅音。既而盛德有邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364288_comment'></div>佐皇华而省俗。居群不器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364288_comment'></div>扈輶轩而观风。某疾抱支离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364288_comment'></div>材均臃肿。自弱龄植操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364288_comment'></div>本谢声名。中年誓心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364288_comment'></div>不祈闻达。始则执鞭为仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364288_comment'></div>帝里希干禄之荣。次则捧檄入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364288_comment'></div>私庭庶代耕之乐。然而忠不闻于十室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364288_comment'></div>学无专于一经。退异善交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364288_comment'></div>进殊巧宦。抟羊角而遐翥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364288_comment'></div>浩矣无津。附骥尾以上驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364288_comment'></div>邈焉难托。实欲垂竿投饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364288_comment'></div>晦名迹于渭滨。抱瓮灌园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364288_comment'></div>绝机心于汉渚。幸属乾坤贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364288_comment'></div>乌兔光华。嵩山动万岁之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364288_comment'></div>德水应千年之色。虽无为光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364288_comment'></div>忻预比屋之封。而有道贱贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364288_comment'></div>耻作归田之赋。明公顾盼成饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364288_comment'></div>咳唾为恩。漏微润于江波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364288_comment'></div>流末光于邻烛。幽禽迁木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364288_comment'></div>侣丹山于帝梧。鸣石浮川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364288_comment'></div>应黄钟于仙管。敢布心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364288_comment'></div>讵能望焉。谨启<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364288_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1364288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1364288'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_42_1364288_0'>⑴ 谨桉此据永乐大典本采入与今传本详略互异附载其后灵隐集上梁明府启云昔者闻歌薛邑赏弹铗于冯驩伫驾夷门揖抱关于侯子岂惟成风之斲妙思通神流水之弦清音入听况夫志合者蓬心可采情谐者兰味宁忘伏惟公仪天耸搆层基控射牛之峰浸地开源惊涛疏钓鳌之浦至夫封侯庙食掩金许以霞搴三主八公罩袁杨而岳立于是功超振鹭位典烹鲜水镜澄澜照翔鸾之舞影吟琴动操叶驯雉之雅音既而盛德有邻佐皇华而抚俗君子不器扈輶轩以观风某蒲石橘迁声乡蓬转不叶十室无专一经攀骥逸而无由仰鹏飞而自失公顾盼成饰咳唾为恩庶微润于江波冀末光于邻烛使幽禽迁木侣丹山于帝梧鸣石在川应黄钟于仙管敢布心也讵能望焉谨启</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1364288_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9b04690fbfd2488b82ef86d9db02a43e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9b04690fbfd2488b82ef86d9db02a43e");'><span id='9b04690fbfd2488b82ef86d9db02a43e_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>入京应举.行前,有《上瑕丘韦明府启》、《上郭赞府启》等文求推荐。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第266页。）</span>《上郭赞府启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第271页。）</span><div id='poem_1364278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上瑕邱韦明府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（654年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364278")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364278'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364278'>宾王启。侧闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>戢翮</span>触笼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364278_comment'></div>负垂天而跼影。伏枥羁蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364278_comment'></div>望绝尘而踠足。故以游莲遇绁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364278_comment'></div>悟宋王于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>婴罗</span>。在藻迷波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364278_comment'></div>顾蒙庄于煦辙。是以临淄遣妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364278_comment'></div>寄束缊于齐邻。邯郸下客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364278_comment'></div>效<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>处囊</span>于赵相。伏惟明府公缔址琼峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364278_comment'></div>灵岳蔽丹霄之景。图基珠浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364278_comment'></div>神流沃清汉之波。玉札飞文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364278_comment'></div>综宏词于楚傅。金籯缉艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364278_comment'></div>味雅道于扶阳。孕兰畹而生姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364278_comment'></div>澧灞钟高门之庆。产铜溪而写锷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364278_comment'></div>荆蓝资象德之祯。幼辨羝羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364278_comment'></div>演飞龙之秘策。夙谈孔雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364278_comment'></div>对家禽之丽词。赤野浮衒价之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364278_comment'></div>珠胎莹色。丹穴陪来仪之迅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364278_comment'></div>凤彩含姿。灵襟转璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364278_comment'></div>绚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>逸照</span>于兰池。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>神府</span>惊蘋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364278_comment'></div>韵清音于桂浦。谈丛散馥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364278_comment'></div>韫馀气于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>九兰</span>。笔海飞涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364278_comment'></div>骇洪波于八水。绾铜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>麟甸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364278_comment'></div>制锦凫郊。化洽下车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364278_comment'></div>恩孚揽辔。德声含咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364278_comment'></div>仁风飘十地之雄。道化编谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364278_comment'></div>惠露洒三天之渥。狎中牟之驯雉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364278_comment'></div>岂惧骁媒。惊重泉之瑞鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364278_comment'></div>非关照舞。虽则尘飞范甑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364278_comment'></div>垂银有结绶之华。而乃调理宓弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364278_comment'></div>烹鸡屈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>函牛</span>之量。加以招携白屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364278_comment'></div>劝诱青衿。遂使漱流逸客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364278_comment'></div>望骥足以云蒸。栖泌遗才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364278_comment'></div>款龙门而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>雾会</span>。某纬萧末品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364278_comment'></div>拾艾幽人。寓迹雩坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364278_comment'></div>挹危直之秘说。托根磬渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364278_comment'></div>戢战胜之良图。幸以奉训趋庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364278_comment'></div>束情田于理窟。从师负笈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364278_comment'></div>私默识于书林。至于九流百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364278_comment'></div>颇探其异端。万卷五车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364278_comment'></div>亦研其奥旨。将欲优游三乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364278_comment'></div>负杖以终年。栖迟一邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364278_comment'></div>鸣弦而卒岁。谅以糟糠不赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364278_comment'></div>甘旨之养屡空。箪食无资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364278_comment'></div>朝夕之欢宁展。是以祈安阳之捧檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364278_comment'></div>儗毛义之清尘。思鲁国之执鞭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364278_comment'></div>蹈孔圣之馀志。属以蛬秋应节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364278_comment'></div>雁序戒时。飙金将露玉共清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364278_comment'></div>柳黛与荷缃渐歇。实含毫振藻之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364278_comment'></div>离经析理之期。不揆雕朽之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364278_comment'></div>窃冀迁乔之路。辄期泛爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364278_comment'></div>轻用自媒。傥荆璞无见致疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364278_comment'></div>夜光不逢桉剑。则沈骸九死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364278_comment'></div>终望衔珠。殒首三泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364278_comment'></div>徒希结草。载尘清瞩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364278_comment'></div>跼影外惭。冒渎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364278", 1364278, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>威严</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364278_comment'></div>循心内骇。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364278_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1364278_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上郭赞府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（654年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364287")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364287'>宾王启。侧闻枢精啸谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364287_comment'></div>韵清濑于惊蘋。震德升乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364287_comment'></div>叆元枝而布暖。虽涸鳞濡沬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364287_comment'></div>尚觖望于鲸波。而决羽抢榆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364287_comment'></div>颇思迁于莺树。伏惟公琼基謺秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364287_comment'></div>积珠构于三龙。玉翰惊华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364287_comment'></div>煜瑶林于八桂。仙飞有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364287_comment'></div>萦河泛高尚之舟。德验通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364287_comment'></div>灵策动幽明之镜。产耶溪而濯质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364287_comment'></div>霜镡廓丰匣之姿。孕钟岭而飞华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364287_comment'></div>虹玉绚荆岩之气。松秋表劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364287_comment'></div>翊赪霞而插极。菊晚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>驰芳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364287_comment'></div>涵清露而炫沼。鉴悬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>龙镜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364287_comment'></div>明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>逸照</span>于咸阳。韵入凫钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364287_comment'></div>惊洪音于长乐。心源泛藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364287_comment'></div>控鳌壑以朝宗。情岳披莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364287_comment'></div>掩龟岑而作镇。惠牛曜辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364287_comment'></div>惊荀鹤于谈丛。扬凤摛文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364287_comment'></div>咏邹龙于笔海。故佐铜章于磬渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364287_comment'></div>侧扇文鳐之风。贰墨绶于铜郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364287_comment'></div>赞诱祥鸾之化。弦挥单父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364287_comment'></div>弼清韵于嵇琴。化洽中牟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364287_comment'></div>翊驯翚于潘雉。加以延宾置驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364287_comment'></div>接士轼庐。采拔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>刍微</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364287_comment'></div>迈钦贤于司马。提奖幽滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364287_comment'></div>轶取俊于淳于。某瓮牖轻生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364287_comment'></div>席门贱品。幸以参名比屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364287_comment'></div>悦康衢以自娱。预迹耦耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364287_comment'></div>欣日出而知作。又以家传素业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364287_comment'></div>弋书林而骋志。少奉庭训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364287_comment'></div>驰文圃以游魂。至于白简青箱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364287_comment'></div>颇测探其奥旨。竹书石记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364287_comment'></div>亦幽求其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>邃原</span>。虽未能叫彻帝阍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364287_comment'></div>声驰宰府。而颇亦见推里闬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364287_comment'></div>誉浃乡闾。方今银箭缠秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364287_comment'></div>金壶应节。吮墨翘足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364287_comment'></div>希造杖于一枝。味道弹冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364287_comment'></div>望横经于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>重席</span>。不量庸昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364287_comment'></div>窃冀扬庭。伏乞恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364287_comment'></div>暂垂回盼。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>倘使</span>陈留<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364287", 1364287, "Clauses/79/Comments/1")'>逸调</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364287_comment'></div>下探柯亭之筱。会稽阴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364287_comment'></div>傍眷馀溪之蔡。则回眸之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364287_comment'></div>不独著于前龟。清亮之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364287_comment'></div>谁专称于往笛。虽沧溟远量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364287_comment'></div>敢不愧于牛涔。而嵩岱洪恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364287_comment'></div>终曾酬于蚁垤。轻喧视听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364287_comment'></div>忧詟惟深。猥渎阶庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364287_comment'></div>兢惶交集。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364287_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1364287_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3e86520ffb7b40c08b0f897ff2a66a5b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3e86520ffb7b40c08b0f897ff2a66a5b");'><span id='3e86520ffb7b40c08b0f897ff2a66a5b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=658&endYear=658')">658年</a>，24岁</div><div id='3e86520ffb7b40c08b0f897ff2a66a5b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=658&endYear=658')">658年</a>　迁居长安,家临浐滨.冬,参选,为道王府属,从此进入仕途。作品：《上廉察使启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第262页。）</span><div id='poem_1364286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上廉使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（658年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364286")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364286'>宾王启。每读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364286_comment'></div>见古人负米之情。捧檄之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364286_comment'></div>未尝不废书辍卷。流涕伤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364286_comment'></div>何则。情蓄于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364286_comment'></div>事符则感。形潜于内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364286_comment'></div>迹应斯通。而悦帝力以栖魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364286_comment'></div>情欣养素。仰皇华而畅虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364286_comment'></div>敢用披丹。伏惟公源控玉轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364286_comment'></div>激神涛而涵地。基疏金阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364286_comment'></div>架飞岊以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364286", 1364286, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>韬云</span>。洎乎鹿走周原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364286_comment'></div>霸燕图于即墨。蛇分沛泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364286_comment'></div>封汉爵于华城。福禄攸钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364286_comment'></div>公侯必复。炳灵丹穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364286_comment'></div>习吉黄裳。若乃峰秀学山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364286_comment'></div>列三坟而仰止。澜清笔海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364286_comment'></div>委九流以朝宗。登小鲁之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364286_comment'></div>辩练光于飞马。临大吴之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364286_comment'></div>识宝气于连牛。垂秋实于翰林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364286_comment'></div>绚春花于文苑。清规湛秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364286_comment'></div>照月旦而雕谈。素论凝元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364286_comment'></div>开夜光于妙辩。既而业成麟角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364286_comment'></div>引茅茹而弹冠。道映凤池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364286_comment'></div>绚桃林而曳绶。揆留皇鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364286_comment'></div>忠简帝心。奉职春宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364286_comment'></div>标离光于青殿。代工天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364286_comment'></div>明台耀于紫宸。故得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364286", 1364286, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>龙綍</span>垂光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364286_comment'></div>戢两星而开照。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364286", 1364286, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>鹤盖</span>浮影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364286_comment'></div>翼五云以连阴。某大块流形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364286_comment'></div>小人馀庆。幸河神入昴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364286_comment'></div>映白榆以流祥。江使负图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364286_comment'></div>泛青莲而荐兆。薰风广扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364286_comment'></div>圣日多煇。进不能高议云台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364286_comment'></div>谈社稷之上务。退不能销形地胏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364286_comment'></div>揖箕颍之馀芳。而出没风尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364286_comment'></div>湮沦名利。十年无棣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364286_comment'></div>万里惟桑。既而日远长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364286_comment'></div>出蓬门而西笑。云飘吴会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364286_comment'></div>溯松浦以南浮。冀尘迹邱中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364286_comment'></div>绝汉机于俗网。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364286", 1364286, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>承欢</span>膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364286_comment'></div>驭潘舆于家园。不悟地络遐张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364286_comment'></div>维白驹于空谷。天罗迥布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364286_comment'></div>弋黄鹤于高云。顾巳驽钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364286_comment'></div>并从媒衒。力农贱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364286_comment'></div>未免东皋之劳。反哺私情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364286_comment'></div>遽切南陔之咏。少希顾复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364286_comment'></div>辄布悃诚。虽噬指思归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364286_comment'></div>空轸倚闾之望。而齧臂求仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364286_comment'></div>非图高盖之荣。明公资孝履忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364286_comment'></div>恕己及物。惟几成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364286_comment'></div>论道经邦。庶顾兔离箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364286_comment'></div>动薰风于舜海。从龙润础。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364286_comment'></div>霈甘雨于尧云。则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364286", 1364286, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>白羽书生</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364286_comment'></div>自铭恩于食稻。黄裳童子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364286_comment'></div>将赛德于餐花。拜首回惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364286_comment'></div>倾心霢霂。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364286_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1364286_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ed60104214ad48e9a726d8aedfae5950_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ed60104214ad48e9a726d8aedfae5950");'><span id='ed60104214ad48e9a726d8aedfae5950_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=664&endYear=664')">664年</a>，30岁</div><div id='ed60104214ad48e9a726d8aedfae5950' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=664&endYear=664')">664年7月</a>　秋,为应岳牧举作准备.曾上书司列太常伯右相刘祥道,希望援引。作品：《上司刑太常伯启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷7第225页。陈注本作《上司列太常伯启》）</span><div id='poem_1364280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上司刑太常伯启</a><span class='authorDate'>（664年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364280")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364280'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364280'>侧闻鲁泽祥麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364280_comment'></div>希<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>委质</span>于宣父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364280_comment'></div>吴坂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>逸骥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364280_comment'></div>实长鸣于孙阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364280_comment'></div>是则所贵在乎见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364280_comment'></div>所伸由乎知巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364280_comment'></div>故雕其朴峄山有半死之桐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364280_comment'></div>赏其声柯亭无永枯之竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364280_comment'></div>伏惟太常伯公仪天耸搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364280_comment'></div>横九霄而拓基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364280_comment'></div>浸地开源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364280_comment'></div>控四纪而疏派。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364280_comment'></div>自赤文荐祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364280_comment'></div>曲阜分帝子之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364280_comment'></div>紫气浮仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364280_comment'></div>函谷诞真人之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364280_comment'></div>本支百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364280_comment'></div>君子万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364280_comment'></div>道叶神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364280_comment'></div>黄石授帝师之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364280_comment'></div>德由天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364280_comment'></div>白星降<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>王辅</span>之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364280_comment'></div>峰秀学山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364280_comment'></div>列三坟而仰止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364280_comment'></div>澜清笔海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364280_comment'></div>委四渎以朝宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364280_comment'></div>登小鲁之岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364280_comment'></div>辨练光于曳马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364280_comment'></div>临大吴之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364280_comment'></div>识宝气于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>连牛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364280_comment'></div>垂秋实于谈丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364280_comment'></div>绚春花于词苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364280_comment'></div>辩河飞箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364280_comment'></div>激流翻白马之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364280_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>文江</span>散珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364280_comment'></div>圆波漱骊龙之穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364280_comment'></div>是用德茂麟趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364280_comment'></div>削桐叶以分圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364280_comment'></div>道焕鹤池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364280_comment'></div>映桃花而曳绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364280_comment'></div>既而揆留皇鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364280_comment'></div>忠简帝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364280_comment'></div>奉职春宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364280_comment'></div>烁离光于青殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364280_comment'></div>代工天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364280_comment'></div>明台曜于紫宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364280_comment'></div>综理元风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364280_comment'></div>燮调元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364280_comment'></div>含辉礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364280_comment'></div>皎爱日以流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364280_comment'></div>毓彩文昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364280_comment'></div>映德星而开照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364280_comment'></div>若乃识度宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364280_comment'></div>器宇疏通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364280_comment'></div>明允笃诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364280_comment'></div>盛业隆于后土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364280_comment'></div>惠和忠肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364280_comment'></div>元功格于上天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364280_comment'></div>则伊陟谢其缉熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364280_comment'></div>巫咸惭其保乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364280_comment'></div>举才应器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364280_comment'></div>与士无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364280_comment'></div>水镜澄花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364280_comment'></div>炫金波于灵府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364280_comment'></div>冰壶彻鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364280_comment'></div>朗玉烛于神机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364280_comment'></div>则邓攸莫际其澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364280_comment'></div>卢毓罕窥其术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364280_comment'></div>故使妍媸各安其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364280_comment'></div>轻重不失其权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364280_comment'></div>五教克敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364280_comment'></div>百揆时叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364280_comment'></div>折冲千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364280_comment'></div>鲁连谈笑之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364280_comment'></div>师表一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364280_comment'></div>郭泰人伦之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364280_comment'></div>加以分庭让士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364280_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>虚席</span>礼贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364280_comment'></div>片善经心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364280_comment'></div>揖仲宣于蔡席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364280_comment'></div>一言合道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364280_comment'></div>接然明于郑阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364280_comment'></div>某蓬芦布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364280_comment'></div>绳枢韦带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364280_comment'></div>自弱龄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>植操</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364280_comment'></div>本谢声名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364280_comment'></div>中年誓心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364280_comment'></div>不期闻达。<div id='poem_sentence_89_1364280_comment'></div>次则捧檄入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364280_comment'></div>私室庶代耕之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364280_comment'></div>然而忠不闻于十室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364280_comment'></div>学无专于一经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364280_comment'></div>退异善藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364280_comment'></div>进殊巧宦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364280_comment'></div>抟羊角而高翥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364280_comment'></div>浩若无津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364280_comment'></div>附骥尾以上驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364280_comment'></div>邈焉难托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364280_comment'></div>实欲投竿垂饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364280_comment'></div>晦名迹于渭滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364280_comment'></div>抱瓮灌园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364280_comment'></div>绝机心于汉渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364280_comment'></div>幸属乾坤贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364280_comment'></div>乌兔光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364280_comment'></div>嵩山动万岁之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364280_comment'></div>德水应千年之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364280_comment'></div>虽无为光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364280_comment'></div>欣预比屋之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364280_comment'></div>而有道贱贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364280_comment'></div>耻作归田之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364280_comment'></div>于是朅来瓮牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364280_comment'></div>利见金门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364280_comment'></div>指帝乡以望云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364280_comment'></div>赴长安而就日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364280_comment'></div>美芹之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364280_comment'></div>徒有献于至尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364280_comment'></div>蟠木之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364280_comment'></div>谁为容于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364280_comment'></div>明公决几成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364280_comment'></div>论道经邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364280_comment'></div>一顾之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364280_comment'></div>骀足逾于仙骥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364280_comment'></div>片言之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364280_comment'></div>鱼目轶于灵蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364280_comment'></div>庶望顾兔离箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364280_comment'></div>动薰风于舜海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364280_comment'></div>从龙润础。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364280_comment'></div>霈甘泽于尧云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364280_comment'></div>则脍馀之鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364280_comment'></div>希振鳞于吴水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364280_comment'></div>膳后之豕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364280_comment'></div>翻化龟于鲁津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364280_comment'></div>拜伏阶墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364280_comment'></div>增惧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1364280", 1364280, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>木谷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364280_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_136_1364280_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=664&endYear=664')">664年</a>　又上书少常伯李安期,亦求援引之事。作品：《上李少常伯启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷7第233页。）</span><div id='poem_1364281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上李少常启</a><span class='authorDate'>（664年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364281")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364281'>宾王启。窃惟阴阳作炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364281_comment'></div>化一气以陶甄。天地为炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364281_comment'></div>混万物为刍狗。然则璧轮均照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364281_comment'></div>或流景于莱城。玉烛平分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364281_comment'></div>独翔寒于黍谷。是污隆迭袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364281_comment'></div>荣悴相循。得气者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364281", 1364281, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>繁滋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364281_comment'></div>失时者零落。伏以君侯疏乾激派。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364281_comment'></div>龙门开竹箭之波。镇地横基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364281_comment'></div>鹄翅峙莲花之岭。曜重晖于若月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364281_comment'></div>炳謺彩于非烟。至若瑞动赤符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364281_comment'></div>著元勋于东汉。烽惊紫塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364281_comment'></div>宣武功于北征。奕叶龙光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364281_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364281", 1364281, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>联蝉</span>龟纽。德由天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364281_comment'></div>白星降王辅之精。道叶神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364281_comment'></div>黄石授帝师之略。故得三千运北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364281_comment'></div>击舜海以游鳞。九万图南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364281_comment'></div>望尧云而矫翰。折冲千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364281_comment'></div>鲁连谈笑之功。师表一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364281_comment'></div>郭泰人伦之度。于是九重衔绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364281_comment'></div>悬星彩于宸维。四达埋轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364281_comment'></div>振霜威于权石。加以分庭让士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364281_comment'></div>虚坐礼贤。片善必甄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364281_comment'></div>揖虞翻于东箭。一言可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364281_comment'></div>许顾荣以南金。宾王<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364281", 1364281, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>蟠木朽株</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364281_comment'></div>散樗贱质。墙面难用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364281_comment'></div>灰心易寒。退无毛薛之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364281_comment'></div>进乏金张之援。块然独居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364281_comment'></div>十载于兹矣。然而日夜相代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364281_comment'></div>笑沟壑之非遥。贫病交侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364281_comment'></div>思薜萝而可托。欲乘幽控寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364281_comment'></div>进绮季于青山。乐道栖真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364281_comment'></div>从鲁连于沧海。幸属舜门广辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364281_comment'></div>汉币交驰。遂得伫啸高邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364281_comment'></div>应箕文而动韵。聆吟大野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364281_comment'></div>浮艮岫以流阴。将恐在藻纤鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364281_comment'></div>终寡登龙之望。栖榆弱羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364281_comment'></div>徒仰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364281", 1364281, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>抟鹏</span>之高。所冀曲逮恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364281_comment'></div>资馀润于东里。袭承导引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364281_comment'></div>托轻梦于南柯。抚已多惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364281_comment'></div>循躬增惧。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364281_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1364281_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='765a929ff71d4b048326ab8568bf7dca_label'><a
