ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=670')">666-670年</a>，32-36岁</div><div id='765a929ff71d4b048326ab8568bf7dca' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　对策应举及第,拜奉礼郎,为东台详正学士。作品：《对策文三道》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷9第304页。）</span><div id='poem_1364271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>对策文三道</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364271")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364271'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364271'>问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364271_comment'></div>岱岳游魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364271_comment'></div>入佳城而怛化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364271_comment'></div>瀛洲羽客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364271_comment'></div>竦鹤辔而轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364271_comment'></div>虽则备于缣素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364271_comment'></div>昭晰可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364271_comment'></div>求诸耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364271_comment'></div>虚无罕验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364271_comment'></div>弃杖成龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364271_comment'></div>有异虞翻之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364271_comment'></div>衔恩结草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364271_comment'></div>宁符宗岱之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364271_comment'></div>二者何从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364271_comment'></div>尔其扬搉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364271_comment'></div>对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364271_comment'></div>遐观素论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364271_comment'></div>眇觌元风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364271_comment'></div>惟鬼惟仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364271_comment'></div>难究难测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364271_comment'></div>至夫滕公长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364271_comment'></div>佳城开白日之徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364271_comment'></div>洪崖不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364271_comment'></div>层邱控紫云之盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364271_comment'></div>或祟成苍狗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364271_comment'></div>自是赵王之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364271_comment'></div>道叶赤龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364271_comment'></div>爰通陆安之冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364271_comment'></div>玉垒变苌宏之血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364271_comment'></div>金阙化浮邱之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364271_comment'></div>固能目睹桑田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364271_comment'></div>来作西王之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364271_comment'></div>魂游蒿里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364271_comment'></div>还为北帝之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364271_comment'></div>然而将圣生邹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364271_comment'></div>本忘情于语怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364271_comment'></div>多材封鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364271_comment'></div>亦默论于通仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364271_comment'></div>洎乎大义既乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364271_comment'></div>斯文将坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364271_comment'></div>于是八儒三墨之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364271_comment'></div>异轸分驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364271_comment'></div>九流百家之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364271_comment'></div>殊途竞爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364271_comment'></div>语仙则有无交战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364271_comment'></div>语鬼则虚实相纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364271_comment'></div>遂使结草抗军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364271_comment'></div>爰乖宗岱之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364271_comment'></div>化竹游水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364271_comment'></div>有异虞翻之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364271_comment'></div>然而博访古诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364271_comment'></div>缅寻曩册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364271_comment'></div>徇其浮说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364271_comment'></div>徒有奔竞之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364271_comment'></div>求诸至言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364271_comment'></div>抑匪通经之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364271_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364271_comment'></div>高明瞰室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364271_comment'></div>已著六爻之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364271_comment'></div>太虚游形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364271_comment'></div>式编三洞之箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364271_comment'></div>故齐君出猎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364271_comment'></div>遇豕啼于贝邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364271_comment'></div>周嗣登仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364271_comment'></div>游鹤轩于洛浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364271_comment'></div>况乎干宝硕德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364271_comment'></div>已辑搜神之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364271_comment'></div>刘向通儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364271_comment'></div>非无列仙之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364271_comment'></div>斯皆实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364271_comment'></div>谅匪虚谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364271_comment'></div>谨对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364271_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1364271'>问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364271_comment'></div>士农工商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364271_comment'></div>四民各业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364271_comment'></div>废一不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364271_comment'></div>取譬五材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364271_comment'></div>而阙里致言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364271_comment'></div>鄙于学稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364271_comment'></div>漆园起论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364271_comment'></div>爰称绝机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364271_comment'></div>岂先圣垂文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364271_comment'></div>义有优劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364271_comment'></div>将随方设教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364271_comment'></div>理或变通者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364271_comment'></div>汝其矢陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364271_comment'></div>用启前惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364271_comment'></div>对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364271_comment'></div>出震登皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364271_comment'></div>垂衣裳而驭箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364271_comment'></div>乘乾践帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364271_comment'></div>顺舒惨而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1364271", 1364271, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>字氓</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364271_comment'></div>莫不列九土以开疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364271_comment'></div>因四人而安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364271_comment'></div>故农为政本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364271_comment'></div>两汉举力田之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364271_comment'></div>财用聚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364271_comment'></div>九市列惟金之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364271_comment'></div>陟龙门而就日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364271_comment'></div>入仕弹冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364271_comment'></div>断蝉翼以成风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364271_comment'></div>追工运斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364271_comment'></div>咸用因人成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364271_comment'></div>随利济时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364271_comment'></div>盖五帝通规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364271_comment'></div>三王茂范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364271_comment'></div>然则泣麟上圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364271_comment'></div>训三千以领徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364271_comment'></div>梦蝶幽人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364271_comment'></div>抟九万以齐物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364271_comment'></div>欲使邱门志学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364271_comment'></div>折以问农之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364271_comment'></div>汉渚绝机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364271_comment'></div>抒以灌园之巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364271_comment'></div>斯乃变通权数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364271_comment'></div>趋舍适宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364271_comment'></div>当今海内乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364271_comment'></div>天下乐业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364271_comment'></div>士食旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364271_comment'></div>农服先畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364271_comment'></div>自可孙宏献书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364271_comment'></div>以待公车之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364271_comment'></div>王丹载酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364271_comment'></div>时慰田家之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364271_comment'></div>谨对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364271_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_125_1364271'>问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364271_comment'></div>四十强仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364271_comment'></div>七十悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364271_comment'></div>著在格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364271_comment'></div>存诸甲令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364271_comment'></div>然则颜驷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_130_1364271", 1364271, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>韫价</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364271_comment'></div>殆乎白首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364271_comment'></div>和尊播美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364271_comment'></div>始自龆年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364271_comment'></div>欲使滋泉之彦必臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364271_comment'></div>洛阳之才无舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364271_comment'></div>则堤防或爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364271_comment'></div>襟带徒施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364271_comment'></div>其道如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364271_comment'></div>伫闻嘉答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364271_comment'></div>对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364271_comment'></div>窃闻大人有作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364271_comment'></div>义伫良材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364271_comment'></div>贞士徇名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364271_comment'></div>理资明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364271_comment'></div>是知君必待士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364271_comment'></div>士必待君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364271_comment'></div>故使飞龙在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364271_comment'></div>圣智有贤明之佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364271_comment'></div>巨鱼纵壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364271_comment'></div>元后得唐虞之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364271_comment'></div>然则否泰或爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364271_comment'></div>材运难并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364271_comment'></div>岁渐悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364271_comment'></div>尚牧淄原之豕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364271_comment'></div>年甫志学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364271_comment'></div>且珥汉庭之貂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364271_comment'></div>是知因藉时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364271_comment'></div>和君播元龆之俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364271_comment'></div>当其未遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364271_comment'></div>颜生致白首之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364271_comment'></div>语其古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364271_comment'></div>稽之运会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364271_comment'></div>虽则人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364271_comment'></div>抑亦天时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364271_comment'></div>当今乘六御天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364271_comment'></div>得一居帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364271_comment'></div>翘车<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1364271", 1364271, "Clauses/167/Comments/0")'>猎彦</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364271_comment'></div>束帛旌贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364271_comment'></div>故丛桂幽人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364271_comment'></div>罢韬真于文豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364271_comment'></div>青莲江使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364271_comment'></div>自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_172_1364271", 1364271, "Clauses/172/Comments/0")'>裂兆</span>于非熊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364271_comment'></div>岂止洛阳之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364271_comment'></div>来仪汉国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364271_comment'></div>滋泉之叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364271_comment'></div>降止周朝而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364271_comment'></div>某谈乏二龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364271_comment'></div>识迷三豕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364271_comment'></div>徒以钻木轻焰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364271_comment'></div>仰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_180_1364271", 1364271, "Clauses/180/Comments/0")'>升扶</span>而耀辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364271_comment'></div>化草馀光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364271_comment'></div>对含桂而炫彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364271_comment'></div>回皇如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364271_comment'></div>俯仰多惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364271_comment'></div>谨对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_185_1364271_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　为东台详正学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=669')">668-669年</a>　在东台详正学士任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　以事获罪,罢职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=670&endYear=670')">670年</a>　夏,作《咏怀古意上裴侍郎》献诗裴行俭,求从军自效。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷4第110页。）</span><div id='poem_42174' class='_poem'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42174'>天子未驱策，岁月几沈沦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42174'>轻生长慷慨，效死独殷勤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42174'>徒歌易水客，空老<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(867, "poem_sentence_7_42174")'>渭川人</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42174'>一得视边塞，万里何苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42174'>剑匣胡霜影，弓开汉月轮。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42174'>金刀动秋色，铁骑想风尘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42174'>为国坚诚款，捐躯忘贱贫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42174'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2513, "poem_sentence_12_42174")'>勒功</span>思比宪，决略暗欺陈。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42174'>若不犯霜雪，虚掷玉京春。<div class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>，42岁</div><div id='3a92c346926548f9af576895c3013b13' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为明堂主簿.有《帝京篇》,献裴行俭。作品：《上吏部侍郎帝京篇启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷1第1页。张谱作"京兆府明堂县",今据谭图改"长安"）</span>《帝京篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷1第6页。）</span><div id='poem_1364289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上吏部侍郎帝京篇启</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364289")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364289'>宾王启。昨引注日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364289_comment'></div>垂索鄙文。拜手惊魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364289_comment'></div>承恩累息。楚翚丹质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364289_comment'></div>在荆南以怀惭。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364289", 1364289, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>辽豕白头</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364289_comment'></div>望河东而载恧。宾王散樗易朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364289_comment'></div>蟠本难容。虽少好读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364289_comment'></div>无谢高凤。而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364289", 1364289, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>老不晓事</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364289_comment'></div>有类扬雄。徒以易象六爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364289_comment'></div>幽赞通乎政本。诗人五际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364289_comment'></div>比兴存乎国风。故体物成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364289_comment'></div>必寓情于小雅。登高能赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364289_comment'></div>岂图荣于大夫。盖欲乐道遗荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364289_comment'></div>从心所好。非敢希声刻鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364289_comment'></div>窃誉雕虫。至若资丑行以自媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364289_comment'></div>衒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364289", 1364289, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>庸音</span>而苟进。固立身之殊路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364289_comment'></div>行巳之外篇矣。君侯蕴明略以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364289", 1364289, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>佐时</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364289_comment'></div>虚灵台以照物。观梁父之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364289_comment'></div>识卧龙于孔明。听康衢之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364289_comment'></div>得饭牛于宁戚。是用异人翘首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364289_comment'></div>俊乂归诚。独此疵贱之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364289_comment'></div>谬奉清通之盼。虽仲由之瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364289_comment'></div>终阙响于邱门。而宋玉之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364289_comment'></div>傥均音于郢路。敢忘下里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364289_comment'></div>轻用上呈。庶道叶起予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364289_comment'></div>陈卜商之四始。恐吾几失子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364289_comment'></div>效然明于一言。拜首增惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364289_comment'></div>忧心如醉。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364289_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1364289_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_42176'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_42176", 42176, id='poem_sentence_27_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_42176'>且论三万六千<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作二八千金）</span>是，宁知四十九年非。<div id='poem_sentence_28_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_42176'>古来荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作名）</span>利若浮云，人生<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3145, "poem_sentence_29_42176")'>倚伏</span>信难分。<div id='poem_sentence_29_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_42176'>始见<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8368, "poem_sentence_30_42176")'>田窦</span>相移夺<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作倾代）</span>，俄闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8722, "poem_sentence_30_42176")'>卫霍</span>有功勋。<div id='poem_sentence_30_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_42176'>未厌金陵气，先开石椁文。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_42176'>朱门无复<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10476, "poem_sentence_32_42176")'>张公子</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(235, "poem_sentence_32_42176")'>灞亭谁畏李将军</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_32_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_42176'>相顾百龄皆有待，居然万化咸应改。<div id='poem_sentence_33_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_42176'>桂枝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_42176", 42176, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>芳气</span>已销亡，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(418, "poem_sentence_34_42176")'>柏梁</span>高宴今何在？<div id='poem_sentence_34_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_42176'>春去春来苦自驰，争名争利徒尔为。<div id='poem_sentence_35_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_42176'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(599, "poem_sentence_36_42176")'>久留郎署</span>终难遇，空扫相门谁见知<span class='inlineComment2'>（《纪事》无春去四句）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_36_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_42176'>当时<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作莫矜）</span>一旦擅豪华，自言千载长骄奢。<div id='poem_sentence_37_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_42176'>倏忽抟风生羽翼，须臾失浪委泥沙。<div id='poem_sentence_38_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_42176'>红颜宿昔白头新，脱粟布衣轻故人。<div id='poem_sentence_41_42176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年9;10月</a>　秋冬之际,返长安.旋遭母丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　守孝,居浐滨.与武陟尉员半千书信往来。作品：《答员半千书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第279页。）</span>《叙寄员半千》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷3第99页。）</span><div id='poem_1364274' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364274' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364274?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答员半千书</a><span class='authorDate'>（677年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364274")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364274_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364274'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364274'>张评事至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364274_comment'></div>辱惠书及诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364274_comment'></div>把玩无厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364274_comment'></div>暂如有叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364274_comment'></div>上言离恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364274_comment'></div>下勖交情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364274_comment'></div>笃以猛风乾苏之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364274_comment'></div>弥以骤雨湿薪之喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364274_comment'></div>虽闻义则徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364274_comment'></div>道存于起予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364274_comment'></div>而儗人失伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364274_comment'></div>事均乎玩物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364274_comment'></div>借如诚说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364274_comment'></div>盖足下之不知言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364274_comment'></div>倘或剧谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364274_comment'></div>岂吾人之所仰望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364274_comment'></div>夫鲲之为鱼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364274_comment'></div>潜碧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364274_comment'></div>泳沧流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364274_comment'></div>沈鳃于勃海之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364274_comment'></div>掉尾乎风涛之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364274_comment'></div>而濠鱼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364274", 1364274, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>井鲋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364274_comment'></div>自以为可得而齐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364274_comment'></div>鹏之为鸟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364274_comment'></div>刷毛羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364274_comment'></div>恣饮啄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364274_comment'></div>戢翼于天地之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364274_comment'></div>宛颈乎江海之畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364274_comment'></div>而双凫乘雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364274_comment'></div>自以为可得而亵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364274_comment'></div>及其化羽垂天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364274_comment'></div>抟风九万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364274_comment'></div>振鳞横海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364274_comment'></div>击水三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364274_comment'></div>宁肯借翰于抢榆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364274_comment'></div>假力于在藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364274_comment'></div>资江滨涓流之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364274_comment'></div>待堀堁扬尘之风哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364274_comment'></div>故张子房之达人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364274_comment'></div>击水抟风之适焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364274_comment'></div>朱买臣之屈已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364274_comment'></div>戢翼沈鳃之致焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364274_comment'></div>足下雅得古人之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364274_comment'></div>不乏先贤之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364274_comment'></div>自守庄筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364274_comment'></div>无婴魏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364274_comment'></div>亦宁不知在藻抢榆之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364274_comment'></div>非击水抟风之助哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364274_comment'></div>而词旨殷勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364274_comment'></div>深所未谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364274_comment'></div>盍言尔志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364274_comment'></div>岂若是乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364274_comment'></div>夫人生百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364274_comment'></div>物理千变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364274_comment'></div>名利宠辱之形立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364274_comment'></div>爱憎毁誉之迹生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364274_comment'></div>其有道在则尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364274_comment'></div>德成而上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364274_comment'></div>幽贞为虚白之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364274_comment'></div>静默为太元之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364274_comment'></div>知轩冕是傥来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364274_comment'></div>悟荣华非力致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364274_comment'></div>苟斯道之不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364274_comment'></div>亦何患乎无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364274_comment'></div>而欲图侥倖于权重之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364274_comment'></div>养<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364274", 1364274, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>声誉</span>于众多之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364274_comment'></div>所以杨朱徘徊于岐路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364274_comment'></div>阮籍怵惕于穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364274_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364274_comment'></div>霜往露来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364274_comment'></div>岁寒不待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364274_comment'></div>山高河广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364274_comment'></div>离会无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364274_comment'></div>桂树寒花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364274_comment'></div>公子去而忘返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364274_comment'></div>松岩春草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364274_comment'></div>王孙游以不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364274_comment'></div>去矣员生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364274_comment'></div>远离隔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364274_comment'></div>音尘不嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364274_comment'></div>情其劳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364274_comment'></div>畏途穷谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364274_comment'></div>静躁殊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364274_comment'></div>惠而好我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364274_comment'></div>无密尔音。</div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1364274_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_42144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42144?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_12_42144_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=678&endYear=678')">678年</a>　冬,服除,为长安主簿,旋即迁为侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=678&endYear=678')">678年12月</a>　因受人诽谤贪赃枉法而下狱.作《宪台出絷寒夜有怀》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷4第153页。）</span><div id='poem_42092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宪台出絷寒夜有怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（678年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42092")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42092_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42092'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(584, "poem_allusion_42092")'>南冠</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42092'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42092'>独坐怀明发，长谣苦未安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42092'>自应迷北叟，谁肯问<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_42092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42092'>空馀朝夕鸟，相伴夜啼寒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42145'>覆盆徒望日，蛰户未经雷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' "poem_sentence_17_42145")'>不然灰</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42145'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_42145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_42145'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(42145)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年7月</a>　因受人诽谤贪赃枉法而下狱.初秋,作《萤火赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷6第198页。）</span><div id='poem_1364267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萤火赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（679年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364267")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364267'>余猥以明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364267_comment'></div>久遭幽絷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364267_comment'></div>见一叶之已落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364267_comment'></div>知四运之将终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364267_comment'></div>悽然客之为心乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364267_comment'></div>悲哉秋之为气也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364267_comment'></div>光阴无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364267_comment'></div>时事如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364267_comment'></div>大块是劳生之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364267_comment'></div>小智非周身之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364267_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364267_comment'></div>绨袍非旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364267_comment'></div>白首如新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364267_comment'></div>谁明公冶之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364267_comment'></div>孰辨臧仓之愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364267_comment'></div>是用中宵而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364267_comment'></div>达旦不瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364267_comment'></div>睹兹流萤之自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364267_comment'></div>哀此覆盆之难照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364267_comment'></div>夫类同而心异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364267_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>龙蹲</span>归而宋树伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364267_comment'></div>质殊而声合者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364267_comment'></div>鱼形出而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>吴石</span>鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364267_comment'></div>苟有会于精灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364267_comment'></div>夫何患于异类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364267_comment'></div>况乘时而变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364267_comment'></div>含气而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364267_comment'></div>虽造化之不殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364267_comment'></div>亦昆虫之一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364267_comment'></div>应节不愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364267_comment'></div>信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364267_comment'></div>与物不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364267_comment'></div>仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364267_comment'></div>逢昏不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364267_comment'></div>智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364267_comment'></div>避日不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364267_comment'></div>义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364267_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>临危不惧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364267_comment'></div>勇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364267_comment'></div>事有沿情而动兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364267_comment'></div>因物而多怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364267_comment'></div>感而赋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364267_comment'></div>聊以自广云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364267_comment'></div>伊元功之播气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364267_comment'></div>有丹鸟之赋象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364267_comment'></div>顺阴阳而亭毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364267_comment'></div>资变化而含养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364267_comment'></div>每寒潜而暑至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364267_comment'></div>若知来而藏往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364267_comment'></div>既发挥以外融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364267_comment'></div>亦含光而内朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364267_comment'></div>若夫小暑南收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364267_comment'></div>大火西流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364267_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>林塘</span>改夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364267_comment'></div>云物迎秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364267_comment'></div>忽淩虚而赴远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364267_comment'></div>乍排丛而出幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364267_comment'></div>均火齐之宵映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364267_comment'></div>如夜光之暗投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364267_comment'></div>逝将归而未返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364267_comment'></div>忽欲去而中留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364267_comment'></div>入槐榆而焰发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364267_comment'></div>若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>改燧</span>而环周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364267_comment'></div>绕堂皇而影泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364267_comment'></div>疑秉烛以嬉游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364267_comment'></div>点缀悬珠之网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364267_comment'></div>隐映落星之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364267_comment'></div>乍灭乍兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364267_comment'></div>或聚或散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364267_comment'></div>居无定所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364267_comment'></div>习无常玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364267_comment'></div>曳影周流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364267_comment'></div>飘光淩乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364267_comment'></div>泛艳乎池沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364267_comment'></div>徘徊乎林岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364267_comment'></div>状火井之沈荧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364267_comment'></div>似明珠之出汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364267_comment'></div>值冲飙而不烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364267_comment'></div>逢淫雨而逾焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364267_comment'></div>炤灼兮若湛卢之夜飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364267_comment'></div>的皪兮像招摇之夕烂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364267_comment'></div>与庭燎而相炫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364267_comment'></div>照重阴于已昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364267_comment'></div>共爝火而齐息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364267_comment'></div>避太阳于始旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364267_comment'></div>尔其光不周物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364267_comment'></div>明足自资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364267_comment'></div>偶仙鼠而伺夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364267_comment'></div>对飞蛾之赴熺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364267_comment'></div>类君子之有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364267_comment'></div>入暗室而不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364267_comment'></div>同至人之无迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364267_comment'></div>怀明义以应时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364267_comment'></div>处幽不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364267_comment'></div>居照斯晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364267_comment'></div>随隐显而动息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364267_comment'></div>候昏明以进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364267_comment'></div>委性命兮幽元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364267_comment'></div>任物理兮推迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364267_comment'></div>化<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_99_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>腐木</span>而含彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364267_comment'></div>集<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_100_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>枯草</span>而藏烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364267_comment'></div>不贪热而苟进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364267_comment'></div>每和光而曲全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364267_comment'></div>岂如镕金而自铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364267_comment'></div>宁学膏火之相煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364267_comment'></div>陋蝉蜩之习蜕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364267_comment'></div>怵蝼蚁之慕膻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364267_comment'></div>匪伤蜉蝣之夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364267_comment'></div>不羡龟鹤之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364267_comment'></div>抢榆飞而控地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364267_comment'></div>抟扶起而垂天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364267_comment'></div>虽小大之殊品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364267_comment'></div>岂逍遥之异筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364267_comment'></div>夫何化之斯化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364267_comment'></div>无使然而自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364267_comment'></div>乃若有来斯通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364267_comment'></div>无往不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364267_comment'></div>排朱门而独远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364267_comment'></div>升青云而自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364267_comment'></div>匪偷光于邻壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364267_comment'></div>宁假煇于阳燧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364267_comment'></div>终徇已以效能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364267_comment'></div>靡因人而成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364267_comment'></div>物有感而情动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364267_comment'></div>迹或均而心异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364267_comment'></div>响必应之于同声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364267_comment'></div>道固从之于同类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364267_comment'></div>始未明其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_127_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>趋舍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364267_comment'></div>庸讵识其旨意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364267_comment'></div>子尚不知鱼之为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364267_comment'></div>吾又安能知萤之为利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364267_comment'></div>高明兮有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364267_comment'></div>迁变兮无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364267_comment'></div>牛哀倏而化虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364267_comment'></div>羽泉忽兮生熊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364267_comment'></div>血三年而藏碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364267_comment'></div>魂一变而成虹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364267_comment'></div>知战场之化燐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364267_comment'></div>悟冤狱之为虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364267_comment'></div>彼翾飞之弱质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364267_comment'></div>尚矫翼而淩空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364267_comment'></div>何<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_141_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>微生</span>之多踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364267_comment'></div>独宛颈以触笼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364267_comment'></div>异璧光之照庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364267_comment'></div>同剑影之埋丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364267_comment'></div>觊道迷而可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364267_comment'></div>庶鉴幽而或通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364267_comment'></div>览光华而自照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364267_comment'></div>顾形影以相吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364267_comment'></div>感秋夕之殷忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364267_comment'></div>叹宵行以熠耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364267_comment'></div>熠耀飞兮绝复连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364267_comment'></div>殷忧积兮明且煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364267_comment'></div>见流光之不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364267_comment'></div>怆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_154_1364267", 1364267, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>惊魂</span>之屡迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364267_comment'></div>如过隙兮已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364267_comment'></div>同奔电兮忽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364267_comment'></div>傥馀光之可照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364267_comment'></div>庶寒灰之重然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_158_1364267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年7月</a>　因受人诽谤贪赃枉法而下狱.闻大赦诏,作《在狱咏蝉》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷4第157页。）</span><div id='poem_42079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>在狱咏蝉</a><span class='authorDate'>（679年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42079")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42079_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_42079'>余禁所禁垣西，是法厅事也，有古槐数株焉。虽生意可知，同殷仲文之古树；而听讼斯在，即周召伯之甘棠。每至夕照低阴，秋蝉疏引，发声幽息，有切尝闻。岂人心异于曩时，将虫响悲于前听。嗟乎！声以动容，德以象贤。故洁其身也，禀君子达人之高行；蜕其皮也，有仙都羽化之灵姿。候时而来，顺阴阳之数；应节为变，审藏用之机。有目斯开，不以道昏而昧其视；有翼自薄，不以俗厚而易其真。吟乔树之微风，韵资天纵；饮高秋之坠露，清畏人知。仆失路艰虞，遭时徽纆。不哀伤而自怨，未摇落而先衰。闻蟪蛄之流声，悟平反之已奏；见螳螂之抱影，怯危机之未安。感而缀诗，贻诸知己。庶情沿物应，哀弱羽之飘零；道寄人知，悯馀声之寂寞。非谓文墨，取代幽忧云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_42079_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42079'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(584, "poem_allusion_42079")'>南冠</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42079'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42079'>西陆蝉声唱，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(584, "poem_sentence_0_42079")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_42079", 42079, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>南冠</span></span>客思侵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42079'>那堪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42079", 42079, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>玄鬓</span>影，来对白头吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42079'>露重飞难进，风多响易沈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42079'>无人信高洁，谁为表予心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42079'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_42079'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(42079)'>评注</a><span id='poem_sentence_4_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42181'>五霸争驰千里马，三条竞骛七香车。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42181'>掩映飞轩乘落<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作夜）</span>照，参差步障引<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作列）</span>朝霞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42181'>池中旧水如悬镜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作涵明月）</span>，屋里新妆不让花。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42181'>上苑频经柳絮飞，中园几见<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作番）</span>梅花落。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_42181", 42181, "Clauses/62/Comments/1")'>束<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作策）</span>马</span>，平水且<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_42181", 42181, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>沈牛</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_42181'>华阳旧地标神制，石镜蛾眉真<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作偏）</span>秀丽。<div id='poem_sentence_32_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_42181'>诸葛才雄已号龙，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3404, "poem_sentence_33_42181")'>公孙跃马</span>轻称帝。<div id='poem_sentence_33_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_42181'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2300, "poem_sentence_34_42181")'>五丁</span>卓荦多奇力，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_42181", 42181, "Clauses/69/Comments/1")'>四士</span>英灵富<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作用）</span>文艺。<div id='poem_sentence_34_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_42181'>云气横开八阵形，桥形遥分七星势。<div id='poem_sentence_35_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_42181'>川平烟雾开，游戏锦城隈。<div id='poem_sentence_36_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_42181'>墉<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作墙）</span>高龟望出<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作步转）</span>，水净雁文回。<div id='poem_sentence_37_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_42181'>寻姝入酒肆，访客上琴台。<div id='poem_sentence_38_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_42181'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1006, "poem_sentence_39_42181")'>不识金貂重</span>，偏惜<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2208, "poem_sentence_39_42181")'>玉山颓</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_39_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_42181'>他乡冉冉消年月，帝里沈沈限<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作悠悠恨）</span>城阙。<div id='poem_sentence_40_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_42181'>不见猿声助客啼，唯闻旅思将花发。<div id='poem_sentence_41_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_42181'>我家迢递关山里，关山迢递不可越。<div id='poem_sentence_42_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_42181'>故园梅柳尚馀春<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作有馀）</span>，来时<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作秩）</span>欲言归，执袂怆多违。<div id='poem_sentence_44_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_42181'>北梁俱握手，南浦共沾衣。<div id='poem_sentence_45_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_42181'>别情伤去盖，离念惜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_42181", 42181, "Clauses/93/Comments/1")'>徂<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作光）</span>辉</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_46_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_42181'>知音何所托，木落雁南飞。<div id='poem_sentence_47_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_42181'>回来望<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作卧）</span>平陆，春来酒应熟。<div id='poem_sentence_48_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_42181'>相将菌阁卧<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作望）</span>青溪<span id='poem_sentence_49_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_42181'>十年不调<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作达）</span>为贫贱，百日屡迁随倚伏。<div id='poem_sentence_50_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_42181'>祗为须求<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2698, "poem_sentence_51_42181")'>负郭田</span>，使我再干州县<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作郡）</span>禄。<div id='poem_sentence_51_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_42181'>百年郁郁少<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_42181", 42181, "Clauses/104/Comments/0")'>腾迁</span>，万里遥遥<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作迢迢）</span>入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_42181", 42181, "Clauses/105/Comments/1")'>镜川</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_52_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_42181'>涘<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作吴）</span>江拂潮冲白日<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作浪）</span>，淮海长波接远天。<div id='poem_sentence_53_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_42181'>丛竹凝朝露，孤山起暝烟。<div id='poem_sentence_54_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_42181'>赖有边城月，常伴<span id='poem_sentence_55_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_42181'>东南美箭称吴会，名都隐轸三江外。<div id='poem_sentence_56_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_42181'>涂山执玉应昌期<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作朝）</span>，曲水开襟重文会。<div id='poem_sentence_57_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_42181'>仙镝流音鸣鹤岭，宝剑分辉落蛟濑。<div id='poem_sentence_58_42181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_42181'>未看白马对芦刍，且觉浮云似车盖。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=684')">683-684年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='a98a0f15b16844a59c0c1ee6138141c8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　上长安应岳牧举,然因十二月高宗病故,事寝,骆宾王沉滞于长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　二月,程务挺荐举贤良方正,作《与程将军书》辞之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第296页。）</span><div id='poem_1364273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与程将军书</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364273")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364273'>昨见武郎将。备陈将军之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364273_comment'></div>恩出非常。谈过其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364273_comment'></div>恭闻嘉惠。深用惭惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364273_comment'></div>君侯怀管乐之才。当卫霍之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364273_comment'></div>丰功厚利。盛德在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364273_comment'></div>送往事居。元勋盖俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364273_comment'></div>智足以兴王业。道足以济苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364273_comment'></div>尚且屈公侯之尊。伸筦库之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364273_comment'></div>若下仆者。天地一无用刍狗耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364273_comment'></div>粤自旌贲之辰。即逢圣明之历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364273_comment'></div>材不经务。不能成佐命之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364273_comment'></div>智不通时。不能包周身之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364273_comment'></div>加以天资木强。不能屈节权门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364273_comment'></div>地隔蓬心。不能买名时议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364273_comment'></div>常愿为仁由已。丧我于吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364273_comment'></div>见机可以绝机。无用之为有用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364273_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364273", 1364273, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>随时</span>任其舒卷。与物同其波流者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364273_comment'></div>其于木也。鲁班无所措其钩绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364273_comment'></div>其于驾也。伯乐无所施其衔策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364273_comment'></div>不悟圣朝发明扬之诏。君侯缉雍熙之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364273_comment'></div>曲垂提奖。广借<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364273", 1364273, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>游扬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364273_comment'></div>猥以樗栎之姿。忝预贤良之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364273_comment'></div>当今鸿都富学。麟阁多英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364273_comment'></div>非游夏不可以升堂。非夔牙不可以击节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364273_comment'></div>倘片言失德。事暴区中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364273_comment'></div>匹夫窃议。语流天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364273_comment'></div>进乖得贤之举。退贻薄德之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364273_comment'></div>恐不肖之躯。为高明之累耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364273_comment'></div>必能一盼增价。九术先登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364273_comment'></div>燕昭为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364273", 1364273, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>市骏</span>之资。郭隗居礼贤之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364273_comment'></div>则当效驽骀之用。饰固陋之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364273_comment'></div>陶铸尧舜之典谟。宪章文武之道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364273_comment'></div>上以究三才之能事。下以通万物之幽情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364273_comment'></div>将使词翰为行已外篇。文章是立身岐路耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364273_comment'></div>又何足道哉。言而不惭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364273_comment'></div>恃惠子之知我也。所恨禁门清切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364273_comment'></div>造别无缘。官守牵缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364273_comment'></div>程期有限。某尚期辞满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364273_comment'></div>倘泛孤舟。万里烟波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364273_comment'></div>举目有江河之限。百龄心事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364273_comment'></div>劳生无晷刻之欢。嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364273_comment'></div>流水不穷。浮云自远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364273_comment'></div>沾襟此别。把袂何时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364273_comment'></div>恃以平生之私。忘其贵贱之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364273_comment'></div>幸勿为过。谨不多谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364273_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1364273_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

洛阳

-----title
南召（南阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3b9b42bb9247420daf02d1652e5ef758_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3b9b42bb9247420daf02d1652e5ef758");'><span id='3b9b42bb9247420daf02d1652e5ef758_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=655&endYear=655')">655年</a>，21岁</div><div id='3b9b42bb9247420daf02d1652e5ef758' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=655&endYear=655')">655年</a>　应举落第,南归义乌.途经鲁阳关,作《至分水戍》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷2第56页。张谱未言"汝州",据谭图补。）</span><div id='poem_42082' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42082' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42082?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至分水戍</a><span class='authorDate'>（655年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42082")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42082_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42082'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42082'>行役忽离忧，复此怆分流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42082_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42082'>溅石<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42082", 42082, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>回湍</span>咽，萦丛曲涧幽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42082_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42082'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_42082", 42082, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>阴岩</span>常结晦，宿莽竞含秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42082_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42082'>况乃霜晨早，寒风入戍楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42082_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42082'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42082_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
南阳
-----detail

onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1367, "poem_sentence_3_42117")'>系日</span>光斜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42117'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42117_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
滑县（滑州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='700c11e4a7f34b5184288b2ed744023c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("700c11e4a7f34b5184288b2ed744023c");'><span id='700c11e4a7f34b5184288b2ed744023c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=659&endYear=659')">659年</a>，25岁</div><div id='700c11e4a7f34b5184288b2ed744023c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=659&endYear=659')">659年</a>　为道王府属.随道王李元庆在滑州任.有《秋日饯陆道士陈文林得风字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷2第67页。）</span><div id='poem_42094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋日饯陆道士陈文林</a><span class='authorDate'>（659年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42094")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42094_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_42094'>陆道士将游西辅，通庄指浮气之关；陈文林言返东吴，修途走落星之浦。于是维舟锦水，藉兰若以开筵；绁骑金堤，泛榴花于祖道。于时赤烟沈节，青女司晨，霜雁衔芦，举宾行而候气，寒蝉噪柳，带凉序以含情。加以山接太行，耸羊肠而飞盖；河通少海，疏马颊以开澜，登高切送归之情，临水感逝川之叹，既而嗟别路之难驻。惜离尊之易倾，虽漆园筌蹄，已忘然于道术（已忘言于道术）。而陟阳风雨，尚抒情于咏歌，各赋一言，同为四韵，庶几别后，有畅离忧云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_42094_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42094'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1668, "poem_allusion_42094")'>赤马</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2228, "poem_allusion_42094")'>青牛</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9486, "poem_allusion_42094")'>玄度月</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42094'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42094'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2228, "poem_sentence_0_42094")'>青牛</span>游华岳，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1668, "poem_sentence_0_42094")'>赤马</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作鸟）</span>走吴宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42094'>玉柱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42094", 42094, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>离鸿</span>怨，金罍浮蚁空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42094'>日霁崤陵雨，尘起洛阳风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42094'>唯当<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9486, "poem_sentence_3_42094")'>玄度月</span>，千里与君同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42094'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42094_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
徐州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='502c14aff3ad4c46af6cc7c285f548b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("502c14aff3ad4c46af6cc7c285f548b5");'><span id='502c14aff3ad4c46af6cc7c285f548b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=660&endYear=661')">660-661年</a>，26-27岁</div><div id='502c14aff3ad4c46af6cc7c285f548b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=660&endYear=660')">660年</a>　为道王府属,随道王在徐州.入道王府三年,道王令自状所能,陈《自叙状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷9第301页。）</span><div id='poem_1364270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364270?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自叙状</a><span class='authorDate'>（660年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364270")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364270_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364270'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364270'>伏奉恩旨。令通状自叙所能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364270_comment'></div>某本江东布衣也。幸属大炉贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364270_comment'></div>合璧光辉。易彼上农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364270_comment'></div>叨兹下秩。于今三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364270_comment'></div>然而进不能谈社稷之务。立事寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364270_comment'></div>退不能扫丞相之门。买名天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364270_comment'></div>徒以黄离元吉。白贲幽贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364270_comment'></div>沐少海之波澜。照重光之丽景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364270_comment'></div>虽任能尚齿。载宏进善之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364270_comment'></div>而观过知人。异降自媒之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364270_comment'></div>是用披诚沥恳。以抒愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364270_comment'></div>若乃忘大易之谦光。矜小人之丑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364270_comment'></div>弹冠入仕。解褐登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364270_comment'></div>饰怀禄之心。效当年之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364270_comment'></div>莫不徇名养素。励朽磨铅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364270_comment'></div>自谓身负管乐之资。志怀周召之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364270_comment'></div>若斯人者。可胜道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364270_comment'></div>而修誉察能。听言观行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364270_comment'></div>舍真筌而择士。沿虚谈以取才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364270_comment'></div>将恐有其语而无其人。得其宾而丧其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364270_comment'></div>故曰知人不易。人不易知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364270_comment'></div>抑又闻之。知臣莫若君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364270_comment'></div>知子莫若父。诚能简材试剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364270_comment'></div>考绩求功。观其所由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364270_comment'></div>察其所以。临大节而不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364270_comment'></div>处至公而不可干。冀斯言之无亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364270_comment'></div>于从政乎何有。若乃脂韦其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364270_comment'></div>乾没其心。说已之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364270_comment'></div>言身之善。腼容冒进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364270_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364270", 1364270, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>贪禄</span>要君。上以紊国家之大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364270_comment'></div>下以渎狷介之高节。此凶人以为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364270_comment'></div>况吉士之为荣乎。所以令衒其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364270_comment'></div>斯不奉令。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364270_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1364270_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=661&endYear=661')">661年</a>　为道王府属,随道王在徐州。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
济南（齐州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d401dd33bfd54ed48854404ae98a8c34_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d401dd33bfd54ed48854404ae98a8c34");'><span id='d401dd33bfd54ed48854404ae98a8c34_link'
