0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬,在齐州.作《为齐州父老请陪封禅表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷7第216页。）</span><div id='poem_1364269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为齐州父老请陪封禅表</a><span class='authorDate'>（665年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364269")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364269_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364269'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364269'>臣闻元天列象。紫宫通北极之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364269_comment'></div>大帝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>凝图</span>。宏猷畅东巡之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364269_comment'></div>是知道隆光宅。既辑玉于云台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364269_comment'></div>业绍禋宗。必<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>涂金</span>于日观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364269_comment'></div>陛下乘乾握纪。纂三统之重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364269_comment'></div>御辩登枢。应千龄之累圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364269_comment'></div>故得河浮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>五老</span>。启<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>赤文</span>于帝期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364269_comment'></div>海荐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>四神</span>。奉丹书于王会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364269_comment'></div>瑞开三脊。祥洽五云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364269_comment'></div>既而辑总章之旧文。绍辟雍之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364269_comment'></div>非烟翼驭。移玉辇于梁阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364269_comment'></div>若月乘轮。秘金绳于岱巘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364269_comment'></div>臣等职均刍狗。阴谢桑榆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364269_comment'></div>幸属尧镜多辉。照馀光于连石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364269_comment'></div>轩图光耀。追盛礼于枞金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364269_comment'></div>然而邹鲁旧邦。临淄遗俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364269_comment'></div>俱沐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>二周</span>之化。咸称一变之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364269_comment'></div>境接<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>青畴</span>。俯瞰获麟之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364269_comment'></div>山开翠屺。斜连辨马之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364269_comment'></div>岂可使稷山<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>遗氓</span>。顿隔陪封之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364269_comment'></div>淹中故老。独奉告成之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364269_comment'></div>是用就日披丹。仰璧轮之三舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364269_comment'></div>望云抒素。叫天阍于九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364269_comment'></div>傥允<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>微诚</span>。许陪大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364269_comment'></div>则梦琼馀息。仰仙阙以交欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364269_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364269", 1364269, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>就木</span>残魂。游岱宗而载跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364269_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1364269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬,在齐州。作品：《上齐州张司马启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷7第254页。张谱未言此篇为此年所作.今据骆宾王行迹系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1364285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上齐州张司马启</a><span class='authorDate'>（665年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364285")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364285'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364285_comment'></div>昔者薛邑闻歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364285_comment'></div>揖冯驩于弹铗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364285_comment'></div>夷门命驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364285_comment'></div>顾侯嬴于抱关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364285_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364285_comment'></div>志合风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364285_comment'></div>戴笠均乎乘马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364285_comment'></div>情谐道术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364285_comment'></div>忘筌贵乎得鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364285_comment'></div>是以挹兰言于断金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364285_comment'></div>交蓬心于匪石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364285_comment'></div>庶清音动听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364285_comment'></div>赏流水于牙弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364285_comment'></div>妙思通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364285_comment'></div>叶成风于郢匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364285_comment'></div>伏惟公疏源白水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364285_comment'></div>浸地轴以轮波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364285_comment'></div>纂庆黄轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364285_comment'></div>感星精而诞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364285_comment'></div>缀珠华于七曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364285_comment'></div>联玉叶于五云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364285_comment'></div>至夫神石摛祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364285_comment'></div>灵钩表贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364285_comment'></div>千年驭鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364285_comment'></div>振仙驾于帝乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364285_comment'></div>七叶珥貂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364285_comment'></div>袭荣光于戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364285_comment'></div>固以纷纶国牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364285_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364285", 1364285, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>昭晰</span>家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364285_comment'></div>洎乎鹿走周原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364285_comment'></div>辅秦图而兴霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364285_comment'></div>蛇分<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364285", 1364285, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>沛泽</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364285_comment'></div>翌唐运以开基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364285_comment'></div>常山王之玉润金声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364285_comment'></div>博望侯之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364285", 1364285, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>兰薰桂馥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364285_comment'></div>羽仪百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364285_comment'></div>掩梁窦以霞搴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364285_comment'></div>钟鼎一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364285_comment'></div>罩袁杨而岳立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364285_comment'></div>故得重规远镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364285_comment'></div>湛月路以流清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364285_comment'></div>茂祉遐铺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364285_comment'></div>架云门而擢秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364285_comment'></div>英飞凤穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364285_comment'></div>藻五色以凝华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364285_comment'></div>颖跃龙泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364285_comment'></div>涵九重而毓润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364285_comment'></div>风情疏朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364285_comment'></div>霜明月湛之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364285_comment'></div>气骨端严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364285_comment'></div>雪白冰清之概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364285_comment'></div>若乃性符神授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364285_comment'></div>道擅生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364285_comment'></div>挫三端于情峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364285_comment'></div>朝九流于学海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364285_comment'></div>博闻强识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364285_comment'></div>辩晋国之黄熊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364285_comment'></div>将圣多能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364285_comment'></div>识吴门之白马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364285_comment'></div>言泉漱迥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364285_comment'></div>惊瀑布以飞澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364285_comment'></div>文江澹清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364285_comment'></div>含濯锦而翻浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364285_comment'></div>郁槐市而增茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364285_comment'></div>穆兰室以流芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364285_comment'></div>于是翔鳣应符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364285_comment'></div>观光上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364285_comment'></div>飞龙成卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364285_comment'></div>利见大人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364285_comment'></div>抟羊角以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364285", 1364285, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>垂天</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364285_comment'></div>展骥足而腾景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364285_comment'></div>化贰藩邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364285_comment'></div>绍敬祖之清廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364285_comment'></div>光赞外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364285_comment'></div>陈君回之亮直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364285_comment'></div>推公平而折狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364285_comment'></div>磔鼠谢其严明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364285_comment'></div>拥端悫而字人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364285_comment'></div>化蛇惭其智勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364285_comment'></div>加以清规日举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364285_comment'></div>湛虚照于冰壶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364285_comment'></div>元鉴露凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364285_comment'></div>朗机心于水镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364285_comment'></div>谦光自牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364285_comment'></div>恭巳爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364285_comment'></div>片善必甄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364285_comment'></div>揖虞翻于东箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364285_comment'></div>一言可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364285_comment'></div>许顾荣以南金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364285_comment'></div>某疾抱支离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364285_comment'></div>材均拥肿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364285_comment'></div>进不能握兰分竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364285_comment'></div>绾银黄于云台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364285_comment'></div>退不能绝粒茹芝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364285_comment'></div>炼金丹于地胏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364285_comment'></div>而出没风尘之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364285_comment'></div>沦漂名利之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364285_comment'></div>游无毛薛之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364285_comment'></div>仕乏金张之援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364285_comment'></div>块然独处者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364285_comment'></div>一纪于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364285_comment'></div>然而日夜相代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364285_comment'></div>恐沟壑之非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364285_comment'></div>贫病交侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364285_comment'></div>思薜萝之可托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364285_comment'></div>常愿处幽控寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364285_comment'></div>追夏黄于商山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364285_comment'></div>乐道栖真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364285_comment'></div>从鲁连于沧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364285_comment'></div>岂图语默易爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364285_comment'></div>心迹难并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364285_comment'></div>题桥之恨愈深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364285_comment'></div>攀桂之情徒结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364285_comment'></div>是用绝深乾没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364285_comment'></div>耽阅邱坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364285_comment'></div>谒子将于南荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364285_comment'></div>访康成于北海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364285_comment'></div>西游梁益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364285_comment'></div>效司马王扬之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364285_comment'></div>东入临淄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364285_comment'></div>慕淳于管晏之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364285_comment'></div>瞻言前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364285_comment'></div>徒欲思齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364285_comment'></div>俯惟当今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364285_comment'></div>空劳怀刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364285_comment'></div>不意云浮础润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364285_comment'></div>霜落钟鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364285_comment'></div>揖郭泰于仙舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364285_comment'></div>有道斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364285_comment'></div>赏鬷明于樽俎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364285_comment'></div>盛德犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364285_comment'></div>虽雅调清歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364285_comment'></div>诚寡和于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_133_1364285", 1364285, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>郢路</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364285_comment'></div>而庸音滥吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364285_comment'></div>窃混奏于齐竽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364285_comment'></div>轻撮课囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364285_comment'></div>揄扬盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364285_comment'></div>庶金波离毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364285_comment'></div>零陵之石自飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364285_comment'></div>瑶光建寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364285_comment'></div>萧邱之火渐爇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364285_comment'></div>学惭麟角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364285_comment'></div>德类鸿毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364285_comment'></div>愧汗如浆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364285_comment'></div>忧心若厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364285_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_146_1364285_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

共和（大非川）

"poem_sentence_27_42164")'>沫相濡</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_27_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_42164'>有志惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_42164", 42164, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>雕朽</span>，无庸类散樗。<div id='poem_sentence_28_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_42164'>关山暂超忽，形影叹艰虞。<div id='poem_sentence_29_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_42164'>结网空知羡，图荣岂自诬。<div id='poem_sentence_30_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_42164'>忘情同<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7355, "poem_sentence_31_42164")'>塞马</span>，比德类宛驹。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_42164'>陇阪肝肠绝，阳关亭候迂。<div id='poem_sentence_32_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_42164'>迷魂惊落雁，离恨断飞凫。<div id='poem_sentence_33_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_42164'>春去荣华尽，年来岁月芜。<div id='poem_sentence_34_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_42164'>边愁伤郢调，乡思绕吴歈。<div id='poem_sentence_35_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_42164'>河气通中国，山途限外区。<div id='poem_sentence_36_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_42164'>相思若可寄，冰泮有衔芦。<div id='poem_sentence_37_42164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_42164'></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_42164_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
姚安（姚州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='528bbf98081045f4a2751c0af0e8ed59_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("528bbf98081045f4a2751c0af0e8ed59");'><span id='528bbf98081045f4a2751c0af0e8ed59_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=672&endYear=672')">672年</a>，38岁</div><div id='528bbf98081045f4a2751c0af0e8ed59' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春,在姚州前线,负责军中文字的起草。作品：《兵部奏姚州道破逆贼诺没弄杨虔柳露布》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷10第338页。）</span>《兵部奏姚州破贼设蒙俭等露布》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷10第352页。）</span>《为李总管祭赵郎将文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷10第365页。）</span><div id='poem_1364291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兵部奏姚州破逆贼诺没弄杨虔柳露布</a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364291")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364291'>尚书兵部臣闻北极列象。六合奉天子之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364291_comment'></div>南面乘乾。一统成圣人之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364291_comment'></div>是知衣裳所会。义有辑于殊邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364291_comment'></div>霜露所均。诚兼育于异类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364291_comment'></div>故涂山万国。诛后至者防风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364291_comment'></div>丹浦一戎。缓前禽者就日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364291_comment'></div>然则利弧矢以威天下。法雷霆以靖域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364291_comment'></div>四时行焉。天道不能去杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364291_comment'></div>五兵备矣。皇业所以胜残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364291_comment'></div>虽事切救焚。苟顺时以济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364291_comment'></div>恩深祝网。不获巳而用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364291_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下登翠妫以握图。宪紫微而正象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364291_comment'></div>元功不宰。混太始以凝神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364291_comment'></div>至道无名。伫华胥而得梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364291_comment'></div>阐文教以清中夏。崇武功以制九夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364291_comment'></div>环海十洲。通波太液之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364291_comment'></div>邓林万里。交影甘泉之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364291_comment'></div>反踵穿胸之域。袭冠带以来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364291_comment'></div>奇肱儋耳之酋。奉正朔而请吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364291_comment'></div>逆贼蒙俭和舍等。浮竹遗种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364291_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>沈木</span>馀苗。邑殊礼义之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364291_comment'></div>人习贪残之性。日者王明广烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364291_comment'></div>帝道遐融。颇亦削左衽而被朝衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364291_comment'></div>解椎髻而升华冕。而豺狼有性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364291_comment'></div>枭獍难驯。遂敢乱我天常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364291_comment'></div>变九隆而背诞。负其地险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364291_comment'></div>携七部以稽诛。骚乱边疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364291_comment'></div>敚攘州郡。是用三门授律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364291_comment'></div>长驱无战之师。五月渡泸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364291_comment'></div>深入不毛之地。去月二十一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364291_comment'></div>军次三朏昆崙镇。前后捕得生口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364291_comment'></div>知守捉山羌傍山连结十部蛮首徒五万众。此山即南郡中之巨防也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364291_comment'></div>冈蛮千里。西通大荒之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364291_comment'></div>溪谷万重。南极炎洲之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364291_comment'></div>耸乔林而插汉。阴兔有假道之标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364291_comment'></div>拔崇岩以隐天。阳乌无回翼之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364291_comment'></div>峰危束马。路绝悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364291_comment'></div>贼踞临岱之形。负建瓴之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364291_comment'></div>徵风召雨。猬起蜂飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364291_comment'></div>驱杂种以挺灾。封狐千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364291_comment'></div>肆沈黎而作孽。雄虺九头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364291_comment'></div>臣以为制敌以权。柔远者祇成于德教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364291_comment'></div>伐叛以义。决胜者不在乎干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364291_comment'></div>于是广布朝恩。恭宣帝泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364291_comment'></div>申之以安抚。晓之以存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364291_comment'></div>信重蛮陬。无负<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>黄龙</span>之约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364291_comment'></div>赏隆汉爵。不渝白马之盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364291_comment'></div>而地接冉駹。词屡殚于喻蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364291_comment'></div>俗通槃瓠。声不辍于吠尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364291_comment'></div>臣遣左三军子总管宁远将军前守右骁骑万安府长史折冲都尉上柱国刘会基。率检校果毅骁骑尉井陉县开国男刘元暕等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364291_comment'></div>衔枚远袭。卷甲前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364291_comment'></div>偃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/102/Comments/0")'>危旆</span>而设潜兵。疑从天落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364291_comment'></div>乘间道而掩不备。若出地中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364291_comment'></div>又遣右三军子总管明威将军行右武卫翊府中郎将上柱国高奴弗率左武卫天水府折冲都尉张仁操等。陟南山之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364291_comment'></div>冲其要害之路。又遣左一军子总管前右金吾卫翊府左郎将上柱国孙仁感率卫尉府右果毅都尉王文雅等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364291_comment'></div>陵北山之北。绝其飞走之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364291_comment'></div>贼首领杨虔柳诺没弄诺览斯等。振螳螂之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364291_comment'></div>拒辙当轮。纵蚊蚋之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364291_comment'></div>弥山满谷。刘会基高奴弗孙仁感等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364291_comment'></div>并忠勤克著。知略远闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364291_comment'></div>识明君之重恩。轻生有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364291_comment'></div>提太阿之神剑。视死无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364291_comment'></div>弯弧而凶党土崩。举刃而妖徒瓦解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364291_comment'></div>虽危苕沸鼎。未穷枭首之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364291_comment'></div>救死扶伤。犹致析骸之爨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364291_comment'></div>二十二日。臣遣副总管兼安抚副使定远将军前左骁骑翊府中郎将令狐知通率右武卫良将壮府左果毅都尉韩惠德等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364291_comment'></div>拥貔豹之雄。顺天机而左转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364291_comment'></div>遣管内安抚副使朝议大夫使持节守银州刺史上柱国宜春县开国男李大志率前左武卫静初府右果毅都尉上柱国陈宏义等。驱象犀之卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364291_comment'></div>乘地轴以右回。又遣行军司马朝散大夫守巂州都督府长史上柱国梁待辟率守右金吾卫宜昌府果毅都尉阎文成等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364291_comment'></div>总投石拔距之材。蹈中权而拊其背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364291_comment'></div>又遣前守右威卫龙西府果毅都尉康留买等。腾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>跃铁</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/141/Comments/1")'>喷金</span>之骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364291_comment'></div>犯前茅而扼其喉。臣等率守左卫清宫府左果毅许怀秀等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364291_comment'></div>横玉弩以高临。纵金钲而直进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364291_comment'></div>元云结阵。影密西郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364291_comment'></div>赤茎挥锋。气冲南斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364291_comment'></div>飞尘埃而匝地。白日为之昼昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364291_comment'></div>扫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>氛祲</span>以稽天。沧溟为之晦色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364291_comment'></div>兵交刃接。鸟散鱼惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364291_comment'></div>自卯及申。追奔逐北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364291_comment'></div>斩首千馀级。转战三十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364291_comment'></div>激流膏而为泉。似变苌宏之血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364291_comment'></div>委乱骸而挤壑。若泛鳖灵之尸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364291_comment'></div>既而照尽高舂。云昏乙夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364291_comment'></div>贼乃收集馀众。保据重岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364291_comment'></div>臣度彼游魂。虑其宵遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364291_comment'></div>使三军齐进。四面合围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364291_comment'></div>二十三日。乘鱼烂之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364291_comment'></div>启蛇行之阵。扬麾誓众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364291_comment'></div>杖节训兵。一鼓先登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364291_comment'></div>赏必悬于芳饵。九攻桉律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364291_comment'></div>罪无赦于严诛。五部雄材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364291_comment'></div>三河侠少。或生居燕地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364291_comment'></div>尤工即墨之围。或家本秦人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364291_comment'></div>早习昆明之战。叱咤则江山摇荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364291_comment'></div>慷慨则林壑飞腾。举<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_94_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/189/Comments/0")'>鹏力</span>以扬威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364291_comment'></div>耀犀渠而贾勇。澄氛廓祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364291_comment'></div>回夏景以溃春冰。灭迹扫尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364291_comment'></div>若霜风之捲秋萚。战踰百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364291_comment'></div>时历三朝。前后生擒四千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364291_comment'></div>斩首五千馀级。诺没弄杨虔柳等殒元行阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364291_comment'></div>悬首旌门。蒙俭和舍等委众奔驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364291_comment'></div>脱身挺险。虽复刑以止杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364291_comment'></div>丁壮咸伏于诛夷。礼不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/205/Comments/0")'>重伤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364291_comment'></div>班白必存于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1364291", 1364291, "Clauses/206/Comments/0")'>宽宥</span>。昔魏臣赋蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364291_comment'></div>徒闻蒟酱之奇。汉使开邛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364291_comment'></div>才通竹杖之利。岂若膺紫泥而吊伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364291_comment'></div>指丹徼以临戎。一战而孟获成擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364291_comment'></div>再举而哀牢授首。斯并皇威远畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364291_comment'></div>庙略遐覃。奉元猷以配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364291_comment'></div>徒知帝力。掩皇舆而辟地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364291_comment'></div>岂曰臣功。无任庆快之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364291_comment'></div>谨遣某奉露布以闻。军资器械别簿条上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364291_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_112_1364291_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兵部奏姚州破贼设蒙俭等露布</a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364292")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364292'>臣闻七纬经天。星墟分张翼之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364292_comment'></div>八纮纪地。炎洲限建木之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364292_comment'></div>西距大秦。杂金行而布气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364292_comment'></div>南通交趾。枕铜柱以为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364292_comment'></div>俗带白狼。人习贪残之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364292_comment'></div>河沦赤虺。川多风雨之妖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364292_comment'></div>水积炎氛。山涵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>毒雾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364292_comment'></div>竹浮三节。肇兴外域之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364292_comment'></div>木化<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>九隆</span>。颇为中原之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364292_comment'></div>年将千纪。代历百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364292_comment'></div>郑纯之化不追。孟获之风逾煽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364292_comment'></div>故三年疲众。徒闻定笮之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364292_comment'></div>五月出师。未息渡泸之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364292_comment'></div>然则大人拯物。上圣乘期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364292_comment'></div>法乾坤以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>握枢</span>。体刚柔而建极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364292_comment'></div>知仁义不能禁暴。设刑网以胜残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364292_comment'></div>知揖让不可济时。用干戈而靖乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364292_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下祥摛戴玉。拓地轴以登皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364292_comment'></div>道契书绳。掩天纮而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>践帝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364292_comment'></div>元云入户。纂灵瑞于丹陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364292_comment'></div>苍箓升坛。荐祯图于翠渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364292_comment'></div>垂衣裳以朝万国。崇玉帛而礼百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364292_comment'></div>昭俭防奢。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>露台</span>惜中人之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364292_comment'></div>宣风布政。明堂法上帝之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364292_comment'></div>致群生于太和。登品物于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364292_comment'></div>四神践雪。五老飞星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364292_comment'></div>君囿祥麟。乐班文于仙卉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364292_comment'></div>女床鸣凤。韵归昌于帝梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364292_comment'></div>四隩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>同文</span>。五方异色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364292_comment'></div>邓林万里。才疏苑囿之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364292_comment'></div>曾城九重。未出池隍之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364292_comment'></div>六合照临之地。候月归琛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364292_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>大炉</span>覆载之间。占风纳赆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364292_comment'></div>蠢兹蛮貊。敢乱天常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364292_comment'></div>横赤熛以疏疆。背朱提而设险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364292_comment'></div>山林万仞。岩邑千寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364292_comment'></div>望秦阜以相倾。崤陵失四塞之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364292_comment'></div>对梁山而错峙。剑门成一篑之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364292_comment'></div>自谓绝壤遐方。中外足以迷声教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364292_comment'></div>凭深负固。江山可以逃灵诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364292_comment'></div>不知玉弩垂芒。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>凶水</span>无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/81/Comments/1")'>九婴</span>之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364292_comment'></div>瑶阶舞戚。洞庭有三苗之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364292_comment'></div>臣等谬以散材。忝专分阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364292_comment'></div>自白招乘候。顺秋帝以扬旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364292_comment'></div>绛节临边。通夜郎而解辫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364292_comment'></div>云开巂穴。旆转邛川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364292_comment'></div>峻岐折坂之危。尽忘襟带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364292_comment'></div>滇池漏江之固。曾莫籓篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364292_comment'></div>唯逆贼设蒙俭等。未革狼心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364292_comment'></div>仍怀豕突。陆梁方命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364292_comment'></div>旅拒偷生。城接祠鸡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364292_comment'></div>竟无希于改旦。山多神鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364292_comment'></div>终未息于择音。臣以大帝宣威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364292_comment'></div>有征无战。明王仗顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364292_comment'></div>先德后刑。宏圣泽于中孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364292_comment'></div>缓天诛于大造。庶南薰解愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364292_comment'></div>仰云阙以翔魂。东律变音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364292_comment'></div>扣辕门而顿颡。而祝禽疏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364292_comment'></div>徒开三面之恩。毒虺挻灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364292_comment'></div>逾肆九头之暴。乃鸠集馀众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364292_comment'></div>蚁结凶徒。儋耳椎髻之渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364292_comment'></div>千里雾合。凿齿雕题之孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364292_comment'></div>一呼云屯。淩石菌以开营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364292_comment'></div>拒岩椒而峻垒。崇峦切汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364292_comment'></div>若登藏宝之山。绝壑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>凭霄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364292_comment'></div>似瞰封泥之谷。以前月十七日连营布阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364292_comment'></div>踞险扬兵。东西三十馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364292_comment'></div>马步二十馀万。聚蚊蚋而成响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364292_comment'></div>声若雷霆。纵蛇豕以为群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364292_comment'></div>气冲宇宙。臣遣中郎将令狐智通等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364292_comment'></div>拥拔山超海之师。当其步阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364292_comment'></div>遣银州刺史李大志等。驱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/143/Comments/0")'>跃景</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/143/Comments/1")'>腾云</span>之骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364292_comment'></div>乘其马军。遣巂州都督府长史行军司马梁待辟等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364292_comment'></div>领劲卒三千。绝其飞走之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364292_comment'></div>遣临源府果毅马仁静等。勒精兵九百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364292_comment'></div>断其潜伏之军。臣率行军长史韩馀庆等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364292_comment'></div>负霜戈而直进。指<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/153/Comments/0")'>云阵</span>以长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364292_comment'></div>庶令斩馘七擒。战士挟雷公之怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364292_comment'></div>伏尸百里。蛮夷识天子之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364292_comment'></div>于是三略训兵。五申誓众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364292_comment'></div>先登陷敌。无遗大树之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364292_comment'></div>后拒乱行。必致曲梁之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364292_comment'></div>楚人三户。蜀郡五丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364292_comment'></div>气拥元云。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/167/Comments/0")'>精贯白日</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364292_comment'></div>喑呜则乾坤摇荡。呼吸则林壑沸腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364292_comment'></div>列旗帜以云舒。似长虹之东指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364292_comment'></div>横剑锋而电转。疑大火之西流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364292_comment'></div>刃接兵交。洞胸达腋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364292_comment'></div>自辰踰午。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_88_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/177/Comments/0")'>鱼烂土崩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364292_comment'></div>沸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/178/Comments/0")'>残息</span>于层峰。更切守陴之哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364292_comment'></div>积圆颅于重阜。殆成京观之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364292_comment'></div>唯贼帅夸干。未悟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/183/Comments/0")'>倾巢</span>之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364292_comment'></div>敢怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/184/Comments/0")'>拒辙</span>之心。独率马军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364292_comment'></div>凭川转斗。惊尘乱起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364292_comment'></div>六合为之寝光。杀气相稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364292_comment'></div>四溟由是变色。副总管李大志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364292_comment'></div>忠唯殉国。义则忘躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364292_comment'></div>临危而贞节逾明。制敌而神机独远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364292_comment'></div>丹诚自守。虽九死其如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364292_comment'></div>白刃交前。岂三军之可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364292_comment'></div>投袂则妖徒雾廓。搴旗而逆党冰摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364292_comment'></div>于是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/202/Comments/0")'>乘利</span>追奔。因机深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364292_comment'></div>困兽犹斗。如战廪君之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364292_comment'></div>穷鸟尚飞。如惊杜宇之魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364292_comment'></div>斩甲卒七千馀级。获装马五千馀匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364292_comment'></div>僵尸蔽野。临赤坂而非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364292_comment'></div>流血洒途。视丹徼以何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364292_comment'></div>首领和舍等。并计穷力屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364292_comment'></div>面缚军门。宽其万死之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364292_comment'></div>宏以再生之路。唯蒙俭脱身铤险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364292_comment'></div>负命穷山。顾巢穴而靡依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364292_comment'></div>延<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_111_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/222/Comments/0")'>晷漏</span>其何几。况妖徒革面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364292_comment'></div>徼外非复他人。部落离心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364292_comment'></div>舟中皆为敌国。瞻言枭首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364292_comment'></div>指日可期。凡在归降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364292_comment'></div>随事招抚。与之经始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364292_comment'></div>复其故业。首邱怀恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364292_comment'></div>疑临故国之墟。安堵知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364292_comment'></div>似入新丰之市。然后班师遁水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364292_comment'></div>振旅禺山。建鸿勋于武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364292_comment'></div>畅元猷于文教。庶荒陬袭中邦之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364292_comment'></div>边疆息外户之虞。华封祝尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364292_comment'></div>兆皇基于千载。夷歌颂汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364292_comment'></div>美王泽于三章。宜与夫天帝前星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364292_comment'></div>广赐秦公之册。坤元益地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364292_comment'></div>遥开王母之图。盖亦有云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364292_comment'></div>曾何足纪。斯并元谟广运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364292_comment'></div>庙略<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_127_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/254/Comments/0")'>遐覃</span>。一戎而荒景肃清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364292_comment'></div>再鼓而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1364292", 1364292, "Clauses/256/Comments/0")'>边隅</span>底定。岂臣等提戈擐甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364292_comment'></div>克全百胜之功。仗节扬麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364292_comment'></div>能通九变之策。诣稿街而献旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364292_comment'></div>大帝成规。闻杕杜以劳旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364292_comment'></div>小臣何力。不胜庆快之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364292_comment'></div>谨遣行军司马朝散大夫守巂州都督府长史上柱国梁待辟奉露布以闻。军资器械别簿录上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364292_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_134_1364292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在姚州前线,作《从军中行路难》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷4第134页。）</span><div id='poem_42172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>从军中行路难二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作辛常伯诗）</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42172")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_42172_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_42172_0'>① 一作行军军中行路难，一作军中行路难</div></div></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42172'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(586, "poem_allusion_42172")'>漂梗</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42172'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42172'>君不见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_42172", 42172, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>封狐</span>雄虺自成群，冯深负固结妖氛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42172'>玉玺分兵徵恶少，金坛受律动<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作劝）</span>将军。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42172'>将军<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_42172", 42172, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>拥旄</span>宣庙略，战士横行<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作戈）</span>静夷落。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42172'>长驱一息背铜梁，直指三巴登剑阁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42172'>阁道岧峣起戍楼，剑门遥裔俯灵丘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42172'>邛关九折无平路，江水双源有急流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42172'>征役无期返，他乡岁华晚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42172'>杳杳丘陵出，苍苍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_42172", 42172, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>林薄</span>远。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42172'>途危紫盖峰，路涩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_42172", 42172, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>青泥坂</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42172'>去去指哀牢，行行入不毛。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42172'>绝壁千里<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作重）</span>险，连山四望高。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42172'>中外分区宇，夷夏殊风土。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42172'>交趾枕南荒，昆弥临北户。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42172'>川原绕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作饶）</span>毒雾，溪谷多淫雨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_42172'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_42172", 42172, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>行潦</span>四时流，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_42172", 42172, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>崩查</span>千岁古。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42172'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(586, "poem_sentence_15_42172")'>漂梗</span>飞蓬不自安，扪藤引葛度危峦。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42172'>昔时闻道从军乐，今日方知行路难。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42172'>沧江绿水东流驶，炎洲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_42172", 42172, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>丹徼</span>南中地。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42172'>南中南斗映星河，秦川秦塞阻烟波。<div id='poem_sentence_18_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_42172'>三春边地风光少，五月泸中瘴疠多。<div id='poem_sentence_19_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_42172'>朝驱疲斥候，夕息倦樵歌。<div id='poem_sentence_20_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_42172'>向月弯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_42172", 42172, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>繁弱</span>，连星转太阿。<div id='poem_sentence_21_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_42172'>重义轻生怀一顾，东伐西征凡几度。<div id='poem_sentence_22_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_42172'>夜夜朝朝斑鬓新，年年岁岁戎衣故。<div id='poem_sentence_23_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_42172'>灞城隅，滇池水。<div id='poem_sentence_24_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_42172'>天涯望转积，地际行无已。<div id='poem_sentence_25_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_42172'>徒觉炎凉节物非，不知关山千万里。<div id='poem_sentence_26_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_42172'>弃置勿重陈，征行多苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_27_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_42172'>且悦清笳杨柳曲，讵忆芳园桃李人。<div id='poem_sentence_28_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_42172'>绛节朱旗分白羽，丹心白刃酬明主。<div id='poem_sentence_29_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_42172'>但令一被君王知，谁惮三边征战苦。<div id='poem_sentence_30_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_42172'>行路难<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本下有行路难岐路字）</span>，几千端。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_42172'>无复归云凭短翰，空馀望日想长安<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_32_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_42172'></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_42172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_42172'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_32_42172_0'>⑴ 一本无空馀二字，此篇一本作辛常伯诗</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_42172_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_42173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42173?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（672年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_42173_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42173'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(383, "poem_allusion_42173")'>一叶先穿</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4576, "poem_allusion_42173")'>馀勇</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42173_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42173'>君不见玉关<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_42173", 42173, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>尘色</span>暗边庭，铜鞮杂虏寇长城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42173'>天子按剑徵<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4576, "poem_sentence_1_42173")'>馀勇</span>，将军受脤事横行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42173'>七德龙韬开玉帐，千里鼍鼓垒<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作千重龟垒动）</span>金钲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42173'>阴山苦雾埋高垒，交河孤月照连营。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42173'>连营去去无穷极，拥旆遥遥过绝国。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42173'>阵云朝结晦天山，寒沙夕涨迷疏勒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42173'>龙鳞水上开鱼贯，马首山前振雕翼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42173'>长驱万里詟祁连，分麾三命武功宣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42173'>百发<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_42173", 42173, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>乌号</span>遥碎柳，七尺龙文迥照莲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42173'>春来秋去移灰琯，兰闺柳市芳尘断。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42173'>雁门迢递尺书稀，鸳被相思双带缓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42173'>行路难，行路难，誓令氛祲静皋兰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42173'>但使封侯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_42173", 42173, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>龙额</span>贵，讵<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作颇）</span>随中妇凤楼寒<span class='inlineComment2'>（同辛常伯作）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_42173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_42173'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(42173)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
成都（益州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cd006bd2515641faaf0af2a0f7a0cdb8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd006bd2515641faaf0af2a0f7a0cdb8");'><span id='cd006bd2515641faaf0af2a0f7a0cdb8_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　秋,赴益州大都督府宴.作《于益州李长史宅宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷9第314页。陈注本作《秋日于益州李长史宅宴序》）</span><div id='poem_1364293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋日于益州李长史宅宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364293")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364293'>夫以五岳栖真。杳眇清溪之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364293_comment'></div>六爻贞遁。寂寥沧海之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364293_comment'></div>斯并激俗矫时。独善之风自远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364293_comment'></div>怀材蕴智。兼济之道未宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364293_comment'></div>长史公元牝凝神。虚舟应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364293_comment'></div>得丧双遣。巢由与许史同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364293_comment'></div>宠辱两存。廊庙与山林齐致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364293_comment'></div>乘展骥之馀暇。俯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364293", 1364293, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>沈犀</span>以开筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364293_comment'></div>曲浦澄漪。似对任棠之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364293_comment'></div>芳亭兴洽。如归山简之池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364293_comment'></div>加以秋水盈襟。寒郊满望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364293_comment'></div>洲渚肃而蒹葭变。风露凝而荷芰疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364293_comment'></div>忘怀在真俗之中。得性出形骸之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364293_comment'></div>虽四子讲德。已颂美于中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364293_comment'></div>而五际陈诗。未形言于大雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364293_comment'></div>爰命虚谀。题其序云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364293_comment'></div>弁侧山颓。自有琴歌客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364293_comment'></div>操觚染翰。非无池水助人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364293_comment'></div>盍各赋诗。式昭乐事云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364293_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1364293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　秋,出使西南,在成都.有《冒雨寻菊序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷9第316页。）</span><div id='poem_1364294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冒雨寻菊序</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364294")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364294'>白帝徂秋。黄金胜友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364294_comment'></div>解尘成契。冒雨相邀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364294_comment'></div>问<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364294", 1364294, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>凉燠</span>则鸿雁在天。叙交游则芝兰满室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364294_comment'></div>砌花舒菊。还同载酒之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364294_comment'></div>岸叶低松。直枕维舟之浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364294_comment'></div>参差远岫。断云将野鹤俱飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364294_comment'></div>滴沥空庭。竹响共雨声相乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364294_comment'></div>仰折巾于书阁。行阅飘麰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364294_comment'></div>挹雅步于琴台。坐闻流水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364294_comment'></div>字中蝌蚪。竞落文河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364294_comment'></div>笔下蛟龙。争投学海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364294_comment'></div>珠帘映水。风生曳露之涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364294_comment'></div>锦石封泥。雨湿印龟之岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364294_comment'></div>泛兰英于户牖。座接鸡谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364294_comment'></div>下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364294", 1364294, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>木叶</span>于中池。厨烹野雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364294_comment'></div>坠白花于湿桂。落紫蒂于疏藤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364294_comment'></div>虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364294", 1364294, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>物序</span>足悲。而人风可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364294_comment'></div>姓名于金谷。不谢季伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364294_comment'></div>混心迹于玉山。无惭叔夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364294_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1364294_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　秋,出使西南,在成都.有《艳情代郭氏赠卢照邻》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷4第140页。）</span><div id='poem_42179' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7433, "poem_allusion_42179")'>三峡无猿</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9119, "poem_allusion_42179")'>下山</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42179'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42179'>迢迢芊<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作芋）</span>路望芝田，眇眇函关恨<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作限）</span>蜀川。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42179'>归云已落涪江外，还雁应过洛水瀍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42179'>洛水傍连帝城侧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_42179", 42179, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>帝宅</span>层甍垂凤翼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42179'>铜驼路上柳千条，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4836, "poem_sentence_3_42179")'>金谷园</span>中花几色。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42179'>柳叶园花处处新，洛阳桃李应芳春。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42179'>妾向双流窥石镜，君住三川守玉人。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42179'>此时离别那堪道，此日空床对芳沼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42179'>芳沼徒游比目鱼，幽径还生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_42179", 42179, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>拔心草</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42179'>流风回雪傥便娟，骥子鱼文实可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2667, "poem_sentence_9_42179")'>掷果河阳</span>君有分，货<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作卖）</span>酒成都妾亦然。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42179'>莫言贫贱无人重，莫言富贵应须种。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(779, "poem_sentence_11_42179")'>绿珠</span>犹得石崇怜，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2893, "poem_sentence_11_42179")'>飞燕</span>曾经汉皇宠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42179'>良人何处醉纵横？直如循默守空名。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42179'>倒提新缣成慊慊，翻将<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3500, "poem_sentence_13_42179")'>故剑</span>作平平。<div id='poem_sentence_13_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_42179'>离前吉梦成<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4460, "poem_sentence_14_42179")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_42179", 42179, "Clauses/28/Comments/1")'>兰兆</span></span>，别后啼痕上竹生。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42179'>别日分明相约束，已取宜家成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_42179", 42179, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>诫勖</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42179'>当时拟弄掌中珠，岂谓先摧庭际玉。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42179'>悲鸣五里无人问，肠断三声谁为续。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42179'>思君欲上望夫台，端居懒听将雏曲。<div id='poem_sentence_18_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_42179'>沈沈落日向山低，檐前归燕并头栖。<div id='poem_sentence_19_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_42179'>抱膝当窗看<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_42179", 42179, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>夕兔</span>，侧耳空房听晓鸡。<div id='poem_sentence_20_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_42179'>舞蝶临阶秪自舞，啼鸟逢人亦助啼。<div id='poem_sentence_21_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_42179'>独坐伤孤枕，春来悲更甚。<div id='poem_sentence_22_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_42179'>峨眉山上月如眉，濯锦江中霞似锦。<div id='poem_sentence_23_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_42179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1065, "poem_sentence_24_42179")'>锦字回文</span>欲赠君，剑壁层峰自纠纷。<div id='poem_sentence_24_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_42179'>平江淼淼分清浦，长路悠悠间白云。<div id='poem_sentence_25_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_42179'>也知京洛多佳丽，也知山岫遥亏蔽。<div id='poem_sentence_26_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_42179'>无那<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_42179", 42179, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>短封</span>即疏索，不在长情守<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_42179", 42179, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>期契</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_27_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_42179'>传闻织女对牵牛，相望重河隔浅流。<div id='poem_sentence_28_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_42179'>谁分迢迢经两岁，谁能脉脉待三秋。<div id='poem_sentence_29_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_42179'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_42179", 42179, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>情知</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_42179", 42179, "Clauses/60/Comments/1")'>唾井</span>终无理，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_42179", 42179, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>情知</span>覆水也难收。<div id='poem_sentence_30_42179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_42179'>不复<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9119, "poem_sentence_31_42179")'>下山</span>能借问，更向卢家字<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4580, "poem_sentence_31_42179")'>莫愁</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42179_comment'></div></div><div
