"Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>三山</span>波浪深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42169'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42169", 42169, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>桃实</span>千年非易待，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1153, "poem_sentence_1_42169")'>桑田</span>一变已难寻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42169'>别有仙居对三市，金阙银宫相向起。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42169'>台前镜影伴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_42169", 42169, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>仙娥</span>，楼上箫声<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1565, "poem_sentence_3_42169")'>随<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_42169", 42169, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>凤史</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42169'>凤楼迢递绝尘埃，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_42169", 42169, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>莺时</span>物色正裴回。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42169'>灵芝紫检参差长，仙桂丹花重叠开。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42169'>双童绰约时游陟，三鸟联翩报消息。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42169'>尽言真侣出遨游，传道风光无限极。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42169'>轻花委砌惹裾香，残月窥窗觇幌色。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42169'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_42169", 42169, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>个时</span>无数并<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_42169", 42169, "Clauses/18/Comments/1")'>妖妍</span>，个里无穷总可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42169'>别有众中称黜帝，天上人间少<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_42169", 42169, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>流例</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42169'>洛滨仙驾启遥源，淮浦灵津符远筮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42169'>自言少小慕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_42169", 42169, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>幽玄</span>，只言容易得神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42169'>佩中邀勒经时序，箫里寻思复几年。<div id='poem_sentence_13_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_42169'>寻思许事真情变，二人容华识少选。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42169'>漫道烧丹止七飞，空传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_42169", 42169, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>化石</span>曾三转。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42169'>寄语天上弄机人，寄语河边值查客。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42169'>乍可悤悤共百年，谁使遥遥期七夕。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42169'>想知人意自相寻，果得深心共一心。<div id='poem_sentence_18_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_42169'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_42169", 42169, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>一心一意</span>无穷已，投漆投胶非足拟。<div id='poem_sentence_19_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_42169'>只将羞涩当风流，持此相怜保终始。<div id='poem_sentence_20_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_42169'>相怜相念倍相亲，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_42169", 42169, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>一生一代</span>一双人。<div id='poem_sentence_21_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_42169'>不把丹心比玄石，惟将浊水况清尘。<div id='poem_sentence_22_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_42169'>只言柱下留期信，好欲将心学松蕣。<div id='poem_sentence_23_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_42169'>不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4146, "poem_sentence_24_42169")'>京兆画</span>峨眉，翻向<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1527, "poem_sentence_24_42169")'>成都骋驺引</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_24_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_42169'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2228, "poem_sentence_25_42169")'>青牛</span>紫气度灵关，尺素赩鳞去不还。<div id='poem_sentence_25_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_42169'>连苔上砌无穷绿，修竹临坛几处斑。<div id='poem_sentence_26_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_42169'>此时空床难独守，此日别离那可久。<div id='poem_sentence_27_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_42169'>梅花如雪柳如丝，年去年来不自持。<div id='poem_sentence_28_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_42169'>初言别在寒偏在，何悟春来春更思。<div id='poem_sentence_29_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_42169'>春时物色无端绪，双枕孤眠谁分许。<div id='poem_sentence_30_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_42169'>分念娇莺一种啼，生憎燕子千般语。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_42169'>朝云旭日照青楼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_42169", 42169, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>迟晖</span>丽色满皇州。<div id='poem_sentence_32_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_42169'>落花泛泛浮灵沼，垂柳长长拂御沟。<div id='poem_sentence_33_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_42169'>御沟大道多奇赏，侠客妖容递来往。<div id='poem_sentence_34_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_42169'>宝骑连花铁作钱，香轮骛水珠为网。<div id='poem_sentence_35_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_42169'>香轮宝骑竞繁华，可怜今夜宿倡家。<div id='poem_sentence_36_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_42169'>鹦鹉杯中浮竹叶，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_42169", 42169, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>凤凰琴</span>里落梅花。<div id='poem_sentence_37_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_42169'>许辈多情偏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_42169", 42169, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>送款</span>，为问春花几时满。<div id='poem_sentence_38_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_42169'>千回鸟信说<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_42169", 42169, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>众诸</span>，百过莺啼说长短。<div id='poem_sentence_39_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_42169'>长短<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_42169", 42169, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>众诸</span>判不寻，千回百过浪关心。<div id='poem_sentence_40_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_42169'>何曾举意<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1788, "poem_sentence_41_42169")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_42169", 42169, "Clauses/82/Comments/1")'>西邻玉</span></span>，未肯留情<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6487, "poem_sentence_41_42169")'>南陌金</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_41_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_42169'>南陌西邻咸自保，还辔归期须及早。<div id='poem_sentence_42_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_42169'>为想三春狭斜路，莫辞九折邛关道。<div id='poem_sentence_43_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_42169'>假令白里似长安，须使<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2228, "poem_sentence_44_42169")'>青牛</span>学剑端。<div id='poem_sentence_44_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_42169'>蘋风入驭来应易，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(796, "poem_sentence_45_42169")'>竹杖成龙</span>去不难。<div id='poem_sentence_45_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_42169'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_42169", 42169, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>龙飙</span>去去无消息，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(516, "poem_sentence_46_42169")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_42169", 42169, "Clauses/93/Comments/1")'>鸾镜</span></span>朝朝减容色。<div id='poem_sentence_46_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_42169'>君心不记下山人，妾欲空期上林翼。<div id='poem_sentence_47_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_42169'>上林三月鸿欲稀，华表千年鹤未归。<div id='poem_sentence_48_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_42169'>不分淹留桑路待，秪应直取桂轮飞。<div id='poem_sentence_49_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_42169'></div><div id='poem_sentence_50_42169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_42169'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(42169)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　居蜀地。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
武功
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e5bce6883d4d4cc2b10121b0c66cc4f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e5bce6883d4d4cc2b10121b0c66cc4f9");'><span id='e5bce6883d4d4cc2b10121b0c66cc4f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>，42岁</div><div id='e5bce6883d4d4cc2b10121b0c66cc4f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年4月</a>　春,任武功主簿.吏部侍郎裴行俭欲辟为掌书记,以母老辞,因作《上吏部裴侍郎书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷8第283页。张谱作"雍州畿县",今据谭图改为"京兆府武功"）</span><div id='poem_1364272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上吏部裴侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364272")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364272'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364272'>四月一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364272_comment'></div>武功县主簿骆宾王谨再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364272_comment'></div>奉书吏部侍郎裴公执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364272_comment'></div>易曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364272_comment'></div>书不尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364272_comment'></div>言不尽意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364272_comment'></div>然则理存乎象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364272_comment'></div>非书无以达其微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364272_comment'></div>词隐乎情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364272_comment'></div>非言无以筌其旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364272_comment'></div>仆诚鄙人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364272_comment'></div>颇览前事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364272_comment'></div>每读古书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364272_comment'></div>高堂九仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364272_comment'></div>曾参负北向之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364272_comment'></div>积粟万钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364272_comment'></div>季路起南游之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364272_comment'></div>未尝不废书辍卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364272_comment'></div>流涕沾襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364272_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364272_comment'></div>情蓄于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364272_comment'></div>事符则感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364272_comment'></div>形潜于内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364272_comment'></div>迹应斯通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364272_comment'></div>是用布腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364272_comment'></div>沥肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364272_comment'></div>庶大雅含宏之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364272_comment'></div>矜小人悃款之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364272_comment'></div>惟君侯察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364272_comment'></div>宾王一艺罕称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364272_comment'></div>十年不调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364272_comment'></div>进寡金张之援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364272_comment'></div>退无毛薛之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364272_comment'></div>亦何尝献策干时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364272_comment'></div>高谈王霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364272_comment'></div>衒才扬已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364272_comment'></div>历诋公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364272_comment'></div>不汲汲于荣名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364272_comment'></div>不戚戚于卑位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364272_comment'></div>盖养亲之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364272_comment'></div>岂谋身之道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364272_comment'></div>不图君侯忽垂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364272", 1364272, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>过听</span>之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364272_comment'></div>任以书记之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364272_comment'></div>儗人则多惭阮瑀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364272_comment'></div>入幕则高谢郤超。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364272_comment'></div>昔聂政荆轲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364272_comment'></div>刺客之流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364272_comment'></div>田光豫让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364272_comment'></div>烈士之分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364272_comment'></div>咸以势利相倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364272_comment'></div>意气相许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364272_comment'></div>尚且捐躯燕赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364272_comment'></div>甘死秦韩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364272_comment'></div>今君侯无求于下官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364272_comment'></div>见接以国士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364272_comment'></div>正当陪麾后殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364272_comment'></div>奉节前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364272_comment'></div>贾馀勇以求荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364272_comment'></div>效轻生而答施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364272_comment'></div>而顾逡巡于成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364272_comment'></div>踌蹰于从事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364272_comment'></div>徒以夙遭不造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364272_comment'></div>幼丁闵凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364272_comment'></div>老母在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364272_comment'></div>常婴羸恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364272_comment'></div>藜藿无甘旨之膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364272_comment'></div>松槚阙迁厝之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364272_comment'></div>抚躬存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364272_comment'></div>何心天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364272_comment'></div>故寝食梦想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364272_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364272", 1364272, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>噬指</span>之恋徒深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364272_comment'></div>岁时烝尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364272_comment'></div>崩心之痛罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364272_comment'></div>若仆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364272_comment'></div>固名教中一罪人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364272_comment'></div>何面目以奉三军之士乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364272_comment'></div>况属天伦之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364272_comment'></div>奄踰七月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364272_comment'></div>违膝下之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364272_comment'></div>忽以三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364272_comment'></div>而凶服之制行终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364272_comment'></div>哀疚之情未泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364272_comment'></div>兴言永慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364272_comment'></div>举目增伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364272_comment'></div>夫怨于心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364272_comment'></div>哀声可以应木石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364272_comment'></div>感于情者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364272_comment'></div>至性可以通神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364272_comment'></div>故徐元直指心以求辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364272_comment'></div>李令伯陈情以穷诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364272_comment'></div>上以弃兴王之佐命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364272_comment'></div>下以全奉亲之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1364272", 1364272, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>笃诚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364272_comment'></div>而蜀主不以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364272_comment'></div>晋君待之愈厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364272_comment'></div>此二人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364272_comment'></div>岂贪贫贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364272_comment'></div>恶荣华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364272_comment'></div>厌万乘之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364272_comment'></div>甘匹夫之辱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364272_comment'></div>盖有不得已者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364272_comment'></div>人有乾没为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364272_comment'></div>脂韦成性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364272_comment'></div>舍慈亲之色养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364272_comment'></div>许明主以驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364272_comment'></div>内忘顾复之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364272_comment'></div>外存傅会之眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364272_comment'></div>薄骨肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364272_comment'></div>厚荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364272_comment'></div>苟背恩而自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364272_comment'></div>则君侯何以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364272_comment'></div>且义士期乎贞夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364272_comment'></div>忠臣出乎孝子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364272_comment'></div>既不能推心以奉母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364272_comment'></div>亦安能死节以事人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364272_comment'></div>虽物议之无嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364272_comment'></div>实吾斯之未信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364272_comment'></div>况流沙一去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364272_comment'></div>绝塞千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364272_comment'></div>子迷入塞之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364272_comment'></div>母切倚闾之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364272_comment'></div>就令观以卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364272_comment'></div>仰南薰之不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364272_comment'></div>而使忧能伤人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364272_comment'></div>迫西山而何几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364272_comment'></div>君侯情深锡类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364272_comment'></div>道叶天经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364272_comment'></div>明恕待人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364272_comment'></div>慈心应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364272_comment'></div>傥矜犬马之微愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364272_comment'></div>悯乌鸟之私情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364272_comment'></div>宽其负恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364272_comment'></div>遂其终养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364272_comment'></div>则穷魂有望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364272_comment'></div>老母知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364272_comment'></div>宾王死罪再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_134_1364272_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
苏州

-----title
绍兴（越州）

<div class='label1' id='e1f18b2e4b734b6a9eab8679c83ddcc5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1f18b2e4b734b6a9eab8679c83ddcc5");'><span id='e1f18b2e4b734b6a9eab8679c83ddcc5_link' "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>销氛</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42153'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(437, "poem_sentence_6_42153")'>投笔</span>怀班业，临戎想<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_42153", 42153, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>顾勋</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42153'>还应雪汉耻，持此报<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_42153", 42153, -----title
萧山（永兴）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cd5e930bb4c942a0a15ee3f62b171a40_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd5e930bb4c942a0a15ee3f62b171a40");'><span id='cd5e930bb4c942a0a15ee3f62b171a40_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年7月</a>　七月初,至越州永兴,为宋思礼作《灵泉颂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷6第208页。）</span><div id='poem_1364268' class='_poem'><div class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364268")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364268'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364268'>闻夫元功幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364268_comment'></div>灵心以有德是亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364268_comment'></div>至道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>冥符</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364268_comment'></div>笃行以通神为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364268_comment'></div>若乃天经地义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364268_comment'></div>色养叶于因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364268_comment'></div>夏凊冬温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364268_comment'></div>爱敬宏于锡类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364268_comment'></div>下逮六幽之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364268_comment'></div>上洞三光之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364268_comment'></div>不有至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364268_comment'></div>孰云斯感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364268_comment'></div>有广平宋思礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364268_comment'></div>字过庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364268_comment'></div>皇朝永州刺史昉之适孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364268_comment'></div>户部员外顺之长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364268_comment'></div>伶丁偏露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364268_comment'></div>早丧慈亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364268_comment'></div>永怀鞠养之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364268_comment'></div>长增思慕之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364268_comment'></div>弱不好弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364268_comment'></div>长而能贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364268_comment'></div>趋庭闻诗礼之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364268_comment'></div>亢宗勖曾闵之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364268_comment'></div>事后母徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364268_comment'></div>以至孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364268_comment'></div>北面兴悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364268_comment'></div>泣高堂而咎已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364268_comment'></div>东游下位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364268_comment'></div>欢微禄以逮亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364268_comment'></div>调露二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364268_comment'></div>来佐百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364268_comment'></div>俯就微班之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364268_comment'></div>将申返哺之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364268_comment'></div>苟立身其若斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364268_comment'></div>于从政乎何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364268_comment'></div>时岁亢旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364268_comment'></div>金石行销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364268_comment'></div>远近川原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364268_comment'></div>殆将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>堙绝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364268_comment'></div>浚井皆为汤谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364268_comment'></div>通波尽化污池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364268_comment'></div>太夫人在迟暮之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364268_comment'></div>有温劳之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364268_comment'></div>非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>滥浆</span>不可以适口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364268_comment'></div>非源泉不可以蠲疴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364268_comment'></div>色养既亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364268_comment'></div>忧惶靡䜣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364268_comment'></div>俄而厅阶之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364268_comment'></div>忽有清泉自生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364268_comment'></div>因疏导其源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364268_comment'></div>遂流注不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364268_comment'></div>味甘若醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364268_comment'></div>气冷如冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364268_comment'></div>此邑城控剡山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364268_comment'></div>地连禹穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364268_comment'></div>基址多石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364268_comment'></div>冈阜无津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364268_comment'></div>爰自兴建以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364268_comment'></div>久微穿汲之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364268_comment'></div>非精诚贯于有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364268_comment'></div>纯志浃于无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364268_comment'></div>孰能洽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>冥贶</span>以通幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364268_comment'></div>导灵泉而致养者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364268_comment'></div>昔汉臣忠烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364268_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>穷井</span>飞于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364268_comment'></div>姜妇孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364268_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>潜波</span>移于七里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364268_comment'></div>静惟陈迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364268_comment'></div>彼亦何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364268_comment'></div>萧县尉柳晃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364268_comment'></div>耿介之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364268_comment'></div>道合则金兰若胶漆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364268_comment'></div>情异则轩冕犹埃尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364268_comment'></div>片善可嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364268_comment'></div>朝闻甘于夕死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364268_comment'></div>一诺犹重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364268_comment'></div>黄金贱于白圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364268_comment'></div>以为执友素交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364268_comment'></div>岂轻肥利禄之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364268_comment'></div>赏音达礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364268_comment'></div>宁钟鼓玉帛之云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364268_comment'></div>所耻者没而无称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364268_comment'></div>所贵者存而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364268_comment'></div>徒怀美志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364268_comment'></div>未遇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>良材</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364268_comment'></div>某出赞荒隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364268_comment'></div>涂经胜壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364268_comment'></div>三秋客恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364268_comment'></div>长怀宋玉之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364268_comment'></div>一面交欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364268_comment'></div>暂雪桓谭之涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364268_comment'></div>睹斯水之清泚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364268_comment'></div>感若人之精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364268_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_94_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>见贤思齐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364268_comment'></div>仰圭璋而有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364268_comment'></div>挥毫兴颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364268_comment'></div>镂琬玉以无惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364268_comment'></div>乃作颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364268_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1364268'>粤若稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364268_comment'></div>厥初生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364268_comment'></div>其谁不孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364268_comment'></div>独我难伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364268_comment'></div>义不悖道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364268_comment'></div>仁不遗亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364268_comment'></div>爱敬尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364268_comment'></div>孝弟通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364268_comment'></div>顾我罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364268_comment'></div>因心感至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364268_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>冥契</span>动天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364268_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1364268", 1364268, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>甘泉</span>涌地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364268_comment'></div>泠泠无竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364268_comment'></div>蒸蒸不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364268_comment'></div>曾是我思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364268_comment'></div>永锡尔类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364268_comment'></div>爰有劳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364268_comment'></div>景行芳尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364268_comment'></div>事谐则感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364268_comment'></div>道洽斯亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364268_comment'></div>孝为礼主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364268_comment'></div>名为实宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364268_comment'></div>倘斯文之不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364268_comment'></div>知盛德之有邻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_122_1364268_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临海

-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e40a2f3a2e1a4633952514b614bdb840_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e40a2f3a2e1a4633952514b614bdb840");'><span id='e40a2f3a2e1a4633952514b614bdb840_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>，49岁</div><div id='e40a2f3a2e1a4633952514b614bdb840' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年7月</a>　七月中旬,过七里滩.作《钓矶应诘文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷10第369页。）</span><div id='poem_1364303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钓矶应诘文</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_1364303")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364303'>余以三伏晨行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364303_comment'></div>至七里濑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364303_comment'></div>此地即新安之江口也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364303_comment'></div>有严子陵钓矶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364303_comment'></div>澄潭至清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364303_comment'></div>洞澈见底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364303_comment'></div>往往有群鱼戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364303_comment'></div>历历如水上行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364303_comment'></div>舟人有钓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364303_comment'></div>试取饵投之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364303_comment'></div>或有游而不顾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364303_comment'></div>或有贪而辄吞之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364303_comment'></div>引竿而举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364303_comment'></div>因以获焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364303_comment'></div>其始出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364303_comment'></div>掉尾扬鬐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364303_comment'></div>有若恃力而自免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364303_comment'></div>其少退也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364303_comment'></div>则鼓鳃濡沬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364303_comment'></div>有似屈体而求哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364303_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364303_comment'></div>势牵于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364303_comment'></div>道穷乎我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364303_comment'></div>将欲以下座而歌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364303", 1364303, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>冯子</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364303_comment'></div>又安能中辙而呼庄周哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364303_comment'></div>余乃祝之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364303_comment'></div>猛兽搏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364303_comment'></div>拘于槛阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364303_comment'></div>鸷鸟攫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364303_comment'></div>絷于樊笼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364303_comment'></div>素龟灵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364303_comment'></div>被发河津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364303_comment'></div>白龙神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364303_comment'></div>挂鳞且网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364303_comment'></div>何不泥潜而穴处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364303_comment'></div>何故贪饵而吞钩乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364303_comment'></div>于是放之江流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364303_comment'></div>尽其生生之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364303_comment'></div>时同行者顾诘余曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364303_comment'></div>夫至人之处世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364303", 1364303, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>拟迹</span>而后投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364303_comment'></div>隐心而后动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364303_comment'></div>终始不易其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364303_comment'></div>悔吝不乖其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364303_comment'></div>而吾子沈缗于川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364303_comment'></div>登鱼于陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364303_comment'></div>烹之可以习政术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364303_comment'></div>羞之可以助庖厨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364303_comment'></div>曩求之将何图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364303_comment'></div>今舍之将何欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364303_comment'></div>余笑而应之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364303_comment'></div>圣人不凝滞于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364303_comment'></div>智士必推移于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364303_comment'></div>知几之谓神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364303_comment'></div>含生之谓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364303_comment'></div>殷乙圣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364303_comment'></div>囚于夏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364303_comment'></div>孔某贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364303_comment'></div>畏于匡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364303_comment'></div>以明哲之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364303_comment'></div>尚罹幽忧之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364303_comment'></div>况鳞羽之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364303_comment'></div>能无弋钓之累哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364303_comment'></div>故曩吾有心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364303_comment'></div>恐求之不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364303_comment'></div>今吾无心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364303_comment'></div>既得之而亡求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364303_comment'></div>夫求与舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364303_comment'></div>不亦双美乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364303_comment'></div>烹与羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364303_comment'></div>不亦两伤乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364303_comment'></div>况疗饥者半菽可以充腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364303_comment'></div>为政者一言可以兴邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364303_comment'></div>亦奚必因小鲜而后明三异之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364303_comment'></div>剿大命而后寄一飧之饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364303_comment'></div>擒而不杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364303_comment'></div>可不谓仁乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364303_comment'></div>获而不飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364303_comment'></div>可不谓廉乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364303_comment'></div>且夫垂竿而为事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364303_comment'></div>太公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1364303", 1364303, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>遗术</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364303_comment'></div>形坐磻溪之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364303_comment'></div>兆应渭水之璜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364303_comment'></div>夫如是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364303_comment'></div>将以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1364303", 1364303, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>钓川</span>耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364303_comment'></div>将以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364303", 1364303, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>钓国</span>耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364303_comment'></div>然后知古之善钓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364303_comment'></div>其惟太公乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364303_comment'></div>又有妙于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364303_comment'></div>其惟文王乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364303_comment'></div>夫文王制六合为钩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364303_comment'></div>悬西伯为饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364303_comment'></div>荐之于清庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364303_comment'></div>投之于巨川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364303_comment'></div>一引而获太公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364303_comment'></div>再举而登尚父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364303_comment'></div>由此观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364303_comment'></div>蹲会稽而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_97_1364303", 1364303, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>沈犗</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364303_comment'></div>鲍肆之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364303_comment'></div>踞沧海而负鳌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364303_comment'></div>渔父之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364303_comment'></div>斯并眇小者之所习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364303_comment'></div>安知大丈夫之所钓哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1364303_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a159c13d1878430b857c9e50f71ecd5d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a159c13d1878430b857c9e50f71ecd5d");'><span id='a159c13d1878430b857c9e50f71ecd5d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>，50岁</div><div id='a159c13d1878430b857c9e50f71ecd5d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年9月</a>　秋,辗转至扬州,与徐敬业等共同谋划反武氏之政.九月,兵举,为军中记室.作《代李敬业传檄天下文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷10第329页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　参与徐敬业反武后之事,有《在军登城楼诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈熙晋《骆临海集笺注》上海古籍出版社1985年版卷5第182页。）</span><div id='poem_42052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>在军登城楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21620, "初唐", "骆宾王", "poem_title_42052")'>骆宾王</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_42052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42052'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42052'>城上风威冷，江中水气寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42052'>戎衣何日定，歌舞入长安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42052'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_42052'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(42052)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年11月</a>　十一月,徐敬业兵败,宾王不知所终。<br /></div>
